// Source: Carrier Misroute (CMR) (CMR)_Client Business Rules_2487.cs
// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        thinClient.loading.show();
        thinClient.dismiss.All();
        userParams.customer = this.vm.shipping.customer.value;
        userParams.labelImage = this.vm.labelImage;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference15 = thinClient.today();
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        thinClient.loading.hide();
        this.vm.labelImage = null;


        if (this.vm.shipping.customer.value == 'AMAZON') {
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ConsigneeReference.IsDisabled = true;
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ShipperReference.IsDisabled = true;
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = true;

            if (this.vm.loadValue == 'Return') {
                this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = false;
                //this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = true;
            }
        }

        if((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option')) {
            this.vm.shipping.activePanel = 0;
            this.vm.shipping.panelMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
        }
        this.vm.loadValue = null;
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        clearInterval(this.vm.intervalId);
        thinClient?.loading.hide();
        this.vm.shipping?.loadValue.focus();


        this.vm.labelImage = null;
        this.vm.shipping?.videoModal?.close();
        this.vm.showShipmentPanel = true

        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ConsigneeReference.IsDisabled = false;
        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ShipperReference.IsDisabled = false;
        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = false;
    }

 this.PrePrint = function(doc, localPort, viewModel){
 // WORKAROUND for bug where printer profile doesn't send optional settings
 // attach control string to set defaults to start of document string
 if((doc.DocumentSymbol == 'UPSAPI.UPS.PACKAGE_LABEL.STANDARD') &&
doc.RawData){
 var printerDefaults = "^XA^LH0,0^XSY,Y^MD30^XZ\n";

 doc.RawData[0] = utoa(newraw);
 }

     function CloseAllShippers() {
        debugger;
        
        var getManifestItemsList,getManifestItemsemethod,methodParams,authorizationToken;
        var allOrdersSelectedCarrier = [];
        var allShipperSelectedCarrier,getShipperCarriersmethod,getShipperCarriersmethodParams,CloseAllShippersResponse,CloseAllShippersResults
        
            getShipperCarriersmethod='api/ShippingService/GetShipperCarriers';
            getManifestItemsemethod='api/ShippingService/GetManifestItems';
            authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
            
        
            let selectedValCarrier = AllCarriersList.find(Carriers => Carriers.Id == $("#CarriersList option:selected").val()).Symbol;
           
            $.each(Array(AllShipperList.length), function(i)
            {
                
                 getShipperCarriersmethodParams = {"ShipperId":AllShipperList[i].Id,"CompanyId":userContextDetails.CompanyId};
                 allShipperSelectedCarrier =  $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getShipperCarriersmethod, data: getShipperCarriersmethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
    
               if(allShipperSelectedCarrier.Carriers && allShipperSelectedCarrier.Carriers.length !=0){ 
               
                    methodParams = {"Carrier":selectedValCarrier,"Shipper":AllShipperList[i].Symbol,"SearchCriteria":{"OrderByClauses":[{"FieldName":"ShipDate","Direction":"DESC"}]},"IncludeImported":false,"CompanyId":userContextDetails.CompanyId};
                    getManifestItemsList =  $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getManifestItemsemethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
                    
                   
                    if(getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems && getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length !=0)
                    {
                        debugger;
                      var CloseManifestmethod,methodParams,CloseAllShippersResults
                        CloseManifestmethod='api/ShippingService/CloseManifest';
                         $.each(Array(getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length), function(j)
                          {
                                  
                                  
                                   allOrdersSelectedCarrier.push({"Attributes":getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Attributes,"ShipDate":getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].ShipDate,"Symbol":getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Symbol,"Name":getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Name});
                              });
                              methodParams ={"Carrier":selectedValCarrier,"ManifestItems":allOrdersSelectedCarrier,"Shipper":AllShipperList[i].Symbol,"Print":true,"UserParams":{},"CompanyId":userContextDetails.CompanyId};
                              CloseAllShippersResponse =  $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + CloseManifestmethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
                              allOrdersSelectedCarrier = [];
                    }
               }
               
          
            });
            
            if(CloseAllShippersResponse != undefined)
            {
                    if(CloseAllShippersResponse.ErrorCode==-1){
                            
                             $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').show();
                             $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                             $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                             $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                                 
                             ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
                            
                        }else
                        {
                                CloseAllShippersResults = CloseAllShippersResponse.CloseManifestResults[0].ErrorCode;
                                if(CloseAllShippersResults!=0){
                                    
                                      $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').hide();
                                      $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').show();
                                      $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                                      $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                                      
                                      ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
                                     
                                }else if(CloseAllShippersResults==0){
                                    
                                     $('#divsuccessfulAllShippers').show();
                                     $('#divsuccessfulAllShippersAndAllCarriers').hide();
                                     
                                      ShowAlert('successfulModalCloseShippers');
                                     
                                }
                        }
           }else
           {
                             $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').show();
                             $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                             $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                             $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                                 
                             ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers'); 
                            
           }
                         
       $('#loaderspinnerImg').hide();
       
        
    }

// Source: Clarios (CLRS)_Clarios_Rule_Paperless_2440.cs
// this.Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {
         $('body').on('change', client.shipping.fileInputPaperless, this.vm, paperlessChange);
  
         function paperlessChange(e) {
             var file = e.target.files[0]
             if (file === undefined) {
                e.data.paperless = null;
             }
             else {
                 var reader = new FileReader();
                 reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                 reader.onloadend = function () {
                     e.data.paperless = { fileName: file.name, fileData: this.result.split(',')[1] }
                 }
             }                
         }       
     }

// client.getUserContext() // returns undefined
getUserContext: function () {
            var userContextUrl = this.config.ShipExecServiceUrl.replace('ShippingService', 'usercontext/GET');
            var authorizationToken = this.getAuthorizationToken();
            this.userContext = $.get({
                url: userContextUrl,
                headers: authorizationToken,
                async: false
            }).responseJSON;
        },

// function ClientBusinessRules() // returns constructor-like function defining business rules
function ClientBusinessRules() {
  var index;
  this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
   // alert(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
    var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
     
  };
  
  this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
      var DIUnit = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight.Units;
      var DIWt = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight.Amount;
      var DINote = "Incorrect shipping of Dry Ice can result in fines upward of $75,000 for each violation as well as cancellation of shipping privileges for all of Conagra Brands. Please contact DL-SmallParcelDeliveryService@conagra.com with questions or for specific instructions and restrictions";
   //   alert(DIUnit);
   //   alert(DIWt);
   //   alert(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight));
  for (var index = 0; index < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; ++index) {  
    switch(shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Units) {
      case "LB":
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 5.5) {
            alert(DINote);
            throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
          
        }
      break;
      case "KG":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 2.49476) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      case "G":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 2494.76) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      case "OZ":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 88) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      default:

    }}

    };
  
  
   this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    };
    

   function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
      for (var index in arr) {
          if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
      }
      return '';
  }
}

// this.PageLoaded(loaded) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function (loaded) {
		//debugger;
		if (loaded === '/shipping') {
			// after page sections load, set values
			$(document).ready(function() {
		        $('form[name="shippingForm"]').find('label:contains("Load")').text("Order Number");
		    });

			var generalInterval = setInterval(function () {
				// wait for general pane to load
				var generalControl = $('form[name="generalForm"]');

				if (generalControl.length > 0) {
					clearInterval(generalInterval);
					generalControl.append('<div class="col-md-6">' +
					'<div class="no-left-right-padding form-group" style="left:-1px;"property="custom_markup" model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19" caption="Markup Percentage">' +
					'<label class="markup-padding">Markup Percentage</label>' + 
					'<input id ="custom_markup_id" type="text" class="form-control">' +
					'</div>' +
				 	'</div>');
				}
			}, 50);
		}

	};

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		vmTemp = this.vm;
		
		console.log(vmTemp);

		shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].CommodityClass = "CLASS_65";
		//document.getElementById("autoship_checkbox").checked = false;
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;   // autoship checkbox

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol = "x";
		}

		// clear Markup Percentage
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");

		// set dialog values/events
		$('#newOrderNumber').val('');
		$('#newWeight').val('');
		$('#newWeight').keypress(function(e) {
			// enforce weight mask
			if (!String.fromCharCode(e.which).match(/[0-9.]+/g)) {
				return false;
			}
		})
		$('#newBoxType').change(function() {
			if ($(this).find('option:selected').val() !== '') {
				// show dimensions string if box was selected
				let length = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length;
				let width = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width;
				let height = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height;
				let units = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units === 0 ? "IN" : "CM";
				$('#newDimensions').val(length + "x" + width + "x" + height + " " + units);
				
				if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					$('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"').prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
			else {
				$('#newDimensions').val('');
			}
		});
		$('#newDimensions').val('');
		$('#newDimensions').keyup(function(e) {
			let loadButton = $('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"');
			if (this.value.trim() === '' && vmTemp.loadValue) {
				loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
			}
			else {
				// enforce dimensions mask if entered LxWxH (IN/CM optional)
				let regEx = /(\d+)x(\d+)x(\d+)( IN| CM)?/
				if (!regEx.test(this.value)) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', true);
				}
				else if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
		});

		// show Load Shipment dialog and set focus
		if (!$('#newShipmentDialog').is(':visible')) {
			$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('show');
			$('#newShipmentDialog').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
				$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
			});
		}
	};

// this.PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, params) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, params) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === null) {
			// if box is empty, add custom dimensions from dialog
			let dims = $('#newDimensions').val().trim().split(/x| /);
			if (dims !== null && dims.length >= 3) {
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="length"]').val(dims[0]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="width"]').val(dims[1]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="height"]').val(dims[2]).change();
				
				let index = 1;
				if (dims.length === 4) {
					dims[3] = dims[3].toUpperCase();
					index = (dims[3] === 'IN' ? 1 : 2);
				}
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('select[name="units"] option:eq(' + index + ')').prop('selected', true);
			}
		}

		let oChk = this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20;		// autoship
		if (oChk === true) {
			params.autoship = oChk;
		}

		$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('hide');
		showLoading(true);
	};

// this.PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		debugger;
		let errorMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
		
		if (errorMessage === undefined) errorMessage = "";
		if (errorMessage === null) errorMessage = "";

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === "x") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("No service selected!");
		}
		
		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage === 'validate') {
			//$("#ctl00_cphContent_left_tabs_consignee_tab_consignee_na_ab_ctrl_na_ctrl_validate_addr_btn").click();
			showLoading(false);
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage.substring(0, 4) === "pop:") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage !== '') {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage);
			let errors = ["not found", "already shipped", "too many"];
			if (errors.some(errorText => errorMessage.includes(errorText))) {
				// open Load Shipment dialog
				this.vm.newShipment();
			}
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}

		$("#custom_markup_id").val(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);

		//getWeight();

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship') {
			this.vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// select all services before rate
		setTimeout(function() {
			// check Select All after delay to allow UI update
			vmTemp.isAllServicesSelected = true;
			vmTemp.selectAllServices();
			vmTemp.rate();
		}, 100);
		
	};

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
		console.log("🚀 [PreShip] Starting PreShip function...");
	    shipmentRequest = vmTemp.currentShipment;
		// Validate shipmentRequest and Packages array
		if (!shipmentRequest || !shipmentRequest.Packages || !Array.isArray(shipmentRequest.Packages)) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			//alert("[PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			return;
		}
	
		let validDimensions = [];
	
		console.log(`📦 [PreShip] Processing ${shipmentRequest.Packages.length} package(s)...`);
	
		// Retrieve current package dimensions from vmTemp
		try {
			let currentPackage = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex];
			if (!currentPackage || !currentPackage.Dimensions) {
				console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] vmTemp.currentShipment package or dimensions not found.");
			} else {
				let dims = currentPackage.Dimensions;
				console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Current Package Dimensions from vmTemp: ${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`);
			}
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Unable to retrieve package dimensions from vmTemp.");
		}
	
		// Loop through all packages to validate their dimensions
		for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
			console.log(`🔍 [PreShip] Checking package at index ${i}...`);
	
			let packageData = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
	
			if (!packageData) {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				return;
			}
	
			if (!packageData.Dimensions) {
				console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				return;
			}
	
			let dims = packageData.Dimensions;
	
			// Ensure all dimension values exist and are valid numbers
			if (dims.Length > 0 && dims.Width > 0 && dims.Height > 0) {
				let dimensionString = `${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`; // Always append "0"
	
				// Validate format (three numeric values + "0" at the end)
				let dimParts = dimensionString.split(new RegExp("[x ]"), 4); // Split on 'x' and space
	
				if (dimParts.length === 4 && !isNaN(dimParts[0]) && !isNaN(dimParts[1]) && !isNaN(dimParts[2]) && dimParts[3] === "0") {
					validDimensions.push(dimensionString);
					console.log(`✅ [PreShip] Package ${i} Dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
				} else {
					console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
					//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions.`);
					return;
				}
			} else {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				return;
			}
		}
	
		// Store only valid dimensions in MiscReference5
		if (validDimensions.length > 0) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = validDimensions.join(", ");
			console.log(`✅ [PreShip] All dimensions successfully stored in MiscReference5: ${shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5}`);
		} else {
			console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] No packages had valid dimensions.");
		}
	
		// Retrieve weight and markup values
		userParams.weight = $('div[caption="Weight"]').find('input[name="unitValue_txt"]').val();
		userParams.markup = $("#custom_markup_id").val();
		console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Retrieved weight: ${userParams.weight}, Markup: ${userParams.markup}`);
	
		// Custom code to hide/filter on postship errors - must be started here
		$("<style> .alert-danger { display: none; } </style>").appendTo("head");
		console.log("🚫 [PreShip] Hidden alert-danger elements to prevent UI issues.");
	
		alertInterval = setInterval(function () {
			var errAlert = $('div.alert-danger');
		
			// Filter and show alert
			if (errAlert.length > 0) {
				clearInterval(alertInterval);
				let msg = errAlert.text();
				if (msg.indexOf('-1') === -1 && msg.indexOf('CONNECTSHIP') === -1) {
					errAlert.show();
					console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] PostShip Alert Detected: ${msg}`);
				}
			}
		}, 200);
	
		console.log("✅ [PreShip] Function completed successfully.");
	};

// this.PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== undefined && shipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== 0) {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("Shipping error: " + shipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
		}
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;		// autoship
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");
/**
		labelInterval = setInterval(function () {
			var labelDialog = $('[uib-modal-window="modal-window"]');
		
			// close label popup if displayed after shipping
			if (labelDialog.length > 0) {
				clearInterval(labelInterval);
				$('[uib-modal-window="modal-window"]').find('.modal-header .row button').click();
			}
		}, 20);
*/
		// clear waiting on alert and dialog intervals
		setTimeout(function() {
			clearInterval(alertInterval);
			clearInterval(labelInterval);
		}, 5000);
	};

// PrePrint(doc, localPort, viewModel) // returns undefined
    this.PrePrint = function(doc, localPort, viewModel){
        // WORKAROUND for bug where printer profile doesn't send optional settings
    	// attach control string to set defaults to start of document string
    	if((doc.DocumentSymbol == 'UPSAPI.UPS.PACKAGE_LABEL.STANDARD') && doc.RawData){
        	var printerDefaults = "^XA^LH0,0^XSY,Y^MD30^XZ\n";
        	var oldraw = atou(doc.RawData[0]);
        	var newraw = printerDefaults + oldraw;
        	doc.RawData[0] = utoa(newraw);
    	}
    };

// function appendCSS() // returns undefined
    function appendCSS(){
        var style = document.createElement('style');
        style.innerHTML = 'input:focus, textarea:focus, select:focus{background-color: #ffffcc;}';
        style.innerHTML += 'li.active a.ng-binding { background-color: #dddddd !important; }';
        document.head.appendChild(style);
    }

// function dismissAlertDialog() // returns undefined
    function dismissAlertDialog() {
        $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function(e) {
            $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
        })
    }

// function ajaxGet(url) // returns result from synchronous GET request
    function ajaxGet(url) {
        var result;
        $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: url,
            async: false,
            success: function(response) {
                result = response;
            }
        });
        return result;
    }

// function ajaxPost(url, data) // returns results from synchronous POST request
    function ajaxPost(url, data) {
        var results;
        $.ajax({
            type: 'POST',
            url: url,
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'json',
            data: data,
            success: function(response) {
                results = response;
            },
            error: function (error) {
                results = error.responseText;
            }
        });
        return results;
    }

// function getCustomData(nameAddress) // returns an array of custom data or []
     function getCustomData(nameAddress) {
        if (nameAddress && nameAddress.CustomData) {
            return nameAddress.CustomData;
        }
        return [];
    } 

// function setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) // returns undefined
    function setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) {
        var isInternational = nameAddress.Country != 'US';
        $('[property="Packaging"] select').prop('disabled', isInternational);
        if (isInternational) {
            var packages = shipmentRequest.Packages;
            for (var i = 0; i < packages.length; i++) {
                packages[i].Packaging = 'LETTER';
            }
        }
    }

// function getStateAbbreviation(state) // returns a state abbreviation or the original state value
    function getStateAbbreviation(state)
    {
        var stateFullNameList = { "arizona": "AZ", "alabama": "AL", "alaska": "AK", "arkansas": "AR", "california": "CA", "colorado": "CO", "connecticut": "CT", "districtofcolumbia": "DC", "delaware": "DE", "florida": "FL", "georgia": "GA", "hawaii": "HI", "idaho": "ID", "illinois": "IL", "indiana": "IN", "iowa": "IA", "kansas": "KS", "kentucky": "KY", "louisiana": "LA", "maine": "ME", "maryland": "MD", "massachusetts": "MA", "michigan": "MI", "minnesota": "MN", "mississippi": "MS", "missouri": "MO", "montana": "MT", "nebraska": "NE", "nevada": "NV", "newhampshire": "NH", "newjersey": "NJ", "newmexico": "NM", "newyork": "NY", "northcarolina": "NC", "northdakota": "ND", "ohio": "OH", "oklahoma": "OK", "oregon": "OR", "pennsylvania": "PA", "rhodeisland": "RI", "southcarolina": "SC", "southdakota": "SD", "tennessee": "TN", "texas": "TX", "utah": "UT", "vermont": "VT", "virginia": "VA", "washington": "WA", "westvirginia": "WV", "wisconsin": "WI", "wyoming": "WY", "alberta": "AB", "britishcolumbia": "BC", "manitoba": "MB", "newbrunswick": "NB", "newfoundland": "NF", "northwestterritory": "NT", "novascotia": "NS", "nunavut": "NU", "ontario": "ON", "princeedwardisland": "PE", "quebec": "QC", "saskatchewan": "SK", "yukon": "YT" }
        if (state == undefined) return state;
        if (state.trim().length == 2) return state;
        var stateFullName = state.toLowerCase().replace(/\ /g, '');
        var returnStateAbbreviation = stateFullNameList[stateFullName];
        if (returnStateAbbreviation == undefined) return state;
        return returnStateAbbreviation;
    }

// function singleCheckbox() // returns undefined
    function singleCheckbox() {
        var $checkbox = $(this);
        if ($checkbox.is(':checked') && $checkbox.is('[name]')) {
            // the name of the box is retrieved using the .attr() method
            // as it is assumed and expected to be immutable
            var group = 'input:checkbox[name="' + $checkbox.attr("name") + '"]';

            // the checked state of the group/box on the other hand will change
            // and the current value is retrieved using .prop() method
            $(group).prop('checked', false);
            $checkbox.prop('checked', true);
        }

    }

// client.init() // returns void
        init: function () {          
            String.prototype.addButtonLabel = function(text) {
                var interval = setInterval(function(selector) { 
                    var $element = $(selector);
                    if ($element.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);                        
                        $element.parent().removeClass('col-md-3');
                        $element.parent().addClass('col-md-4'); 
                        $element.wrap('<label class="ng-binding">').after(text);
                    } 
                }, 10, this);
            }
        }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
  this.PageLoaded = function(location)
  {

    if (location == '/shipping')
    {
      $(function()
      {
        $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val('DOCUMENTS');
        $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"]').delegate('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'blur', function(e)
        {
          $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"] button[ng-click="search(nameaddress)"]').trigger('click');
        });
      });
    }

    if (location == '/batchmanager')
    {
      $(document).ready(function()
      {
        $.globalEval('var userContext;');

        $('#batchUpdateTabs').delegate('li', 'click', function(e)
        {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopImmediatePropagation();
          e.stopPropagation();

          var i = $(this).attr('index');
          UIMethods.SwitchToTab(i);
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[required]', 'keydown', function(e)
        {
          $(this).removeClass('has-error');
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkEditBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.EditThisBatch(this);
        });

        $('body').delegate('#checkboxthirdparty', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CheckForThirdPartyBilling();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.UpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCancelBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CancelUpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

      });
    }
  }

// ParseEncodedData(data) // returns Promise resolving to parsed encoded data
      ParseEncodedData: async function(data)
      {
        let deferred = $.Deferred();

        //nothing came back from the server.
        if (!data) deferred.resolve('No data passed to parser');

        let parseResult = $.parseHTML(data.Data || data)[0].textContent;

        //best guess that the return was json.  parse as json and return
        let f = parseResult.slice(0, 1), l = parseResult.slice(-1);
        let bJsonFirst = ((f.indexOf('{') !== -1) || (f.indexOf('[') !== -1));
        let bJsonLast = ((l.indexOf('}') !== -1) || (l.indexOf(']') !== -1));

        if (bJsonFirst && bJsonLast) { deferred.resolve($.parseJSON(parseResult)) }

        //if the result of the parse was a number, return an integer (may need to change this to a float (++ instead of +)
        //note:  don't parse as float unless you know it's a float.
        //do this in the dev tools console:
        //let pf = '7'; console.log('pf as int', +(pf)); console.log('pf as float', ++(pf));
        //else, return the string
        deferred.resolve($.isNumeric(parseResult) ? +(parseResult) : (parseResult));

        return deferred.promise();
      },

  {

  }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
  this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    ConsolidatedOrders.InitElements(false);
    Tools.HideLoader();
    
    $('#chkDoNotRateShop').prop('checked', shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData3);

// ShowLoader(callback) // returns undefined
      ShowLoader: function (callback)
      {
        $('div.loading').removeClass('ng-hide').addClass('ng-show');

        if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback() };
      },

// HideLoader(callback) // returns undefined
      HideLoader: function (callback)
      {
        $('div.loading').removeClass('ng-show').addClass('ng-hide');
        this.HideOverlay();
      },

// CloseDialogWithoutSaving() // returns undefined
      CloseDialogWithoutSaving: function ()
      {
        $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').empty();
        $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').hide();

        /* HideLoader will hide the loader as well as the overlay. */
        Tools.HideLoader();
      }

// Source: FalconNDX (FNDX)_Falcon_CBR_1794.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) { 
        debugger;
        
        //Days List
        const days = ["Sunday","Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday"];
         
        // Current Date
        var dt = new Date();  
       //dt.setDate(dt.getDate()  +1);
        //alert(dt);
        
        //Finding Last Date of the Month
        var lastDate=new Date(dt.getFullYear(),dt.getMonth()+1 ,0);
        var onlyDate_lastDate= lastDate.getDate();
       
        
          
        //Months List  
        var month= dt.getMonth()+1;
        var nextmonth =dt.getMonth()+1;  //Get the current month
        
        
        //Year
        var currentYear = dt.getFullYear();
  
        
        
                
        var nextdate=dt.getDate()+1;    
        var newdate=dt.getDate()+2;
        
        
        
        /* Comparing current date(saturday/sunday) with lastdate of the month
        1. Current date and last date is saturday 
        2. Next to Current date and last date is saturday */
        
        /* Scenarios
        1. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Sunday 
            Next to current date should match with last date.
        2. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Sunday
            Current date should match with last date.
        3. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Saturday
        4. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Saturday
        
        
        
        */
        
       if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=2;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
       
     
      else if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
              
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
        else if(nextdate == onlyDate_lastDate )  
       {
            
             if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
             
           
       }
       
     //Saturday to Monday 
       var monthIndex = nextmonth;
                if(monthIndex<10)
                monthIndex=('0'+monthIndex);
                
       var mondateIndex=newdate;
                if(mondateIndex<10)
                mondateIndex=('0'+mondateIndex);
                
       var lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
        
     if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
        {
            lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
            $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
        }
         
         
      
      //Sunday to Monday   
         var sundateIndex=dt.getDate();
       
         if(dt.getDate()==onlyDate_lastDate)
            {
              
                 sundateIndex=newdate;   
                   
            }
            else
            {
               
                sundateIndex=dt.getDate()+1;
            }

        
          if(sundateIndex<10)
            sundateIndex=('0'+sundateIndex);
                     
           if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
            {
                 lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+sundateIndex);
                 $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
            }
           
    }

// getAddressBookEntries(addressBookName, context) // returns an array of address book entries or undefined
    function getAddressBookEntries(addressBookName, context) {
        var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Name", FieldValue: addressBookName, Operator: 0 }] };
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
        debugger;
        //var response = ajaxPost('GetAddressBooks', data);
        var response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false);
        debugger;
        if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
            var addressBookEntry = { Code: 'Error: AddressBook "' + addressBookName + '" Not Found' };
            return [addressBookEntry];
        } else {
            var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;

            searchCriteria = { OrderByClauses: [{ FieldName: "Code", Direction: "asc", FieldType: 3 }] };
            data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
            //response = ajaxPost('GetAddressBookEntries', data);
            response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false);
            debugger;
            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) {
                return response.AddressBookEntries;
            }
        }
    }

// Source: FortessaTS (FTS)_FortessaCBR_1897.cs
// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        if (location == '/shipping') this.Shipping();


    }

// this.Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
        //shipperReferenceKeyUp();
        miscReference7KeyUp();
        replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(this.vm.profile.BoxTypes);

        $('body').delegate(client.shipping.addPackageButton, 'keyup', function (e) {

            if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                //client.shipping.shipperReference.focus();
                client.shipping.miscRef7.focus();
            }
        })


        function shipperReferenceKeyUp() {
            $('body').delegate(client.shipping.shipperReference, 'keydown', function (e) {
                if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
                }
            })
        }

        function miscReference7KeyUp() {
            $('body').delegate(client.shipping.miscRef7, 'keydown', function (e) {
                if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
                }
            })
        }


        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        function replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(boxTypes) {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                client.shipping.$selectBoxType = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]');
                if (client.shipping.$selectBoxType.length > 0) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType = $('<input type="text" />').attr({ class: client.shipping.$selectBoxType.attr('class') });
                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.hide();
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.insertAfter(client.shipping.$selectBoxType);

                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.keyup(boxTypes, function (e) {
                        if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                            for (var boxType of e.data) {
                                if (boxType.Name == this.value) {
                                    this.value = '';
                                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.val(boxType.Id).change();
                                    client.shipping.addPackageButton.focus();
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    });

                }
            }, 10);
        }




    }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.getWeight();
		
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

		//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
        //this.vm.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
        //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
		
        //this.vm.overrideOptimization = pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6)
        pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6);
		
		//checkAndSetShipDate(this.vm);
		checkAndSetShipDateTest(this.vm);
		
        this.vm.arriveByDate = client.shipping.arriveByDate;
        client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();

        function pastDueDate(miscReference6) {
            //if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0 && miscReference6 != '*1900-01-01T00:00:00*') {

            if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0) {

                miscReference6 = miscReference6.replaceAll('*', '');
                client.shipping.arriveByDate = miscReference6.split("T")[0];

                var dateRequired = Date.parse(miscReference6);
                if (dateRequired <= Date.now() && miscReference6 != "1900-01-01T00:00:00") {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-success').addClass('text-danger');
                    return true;
                }
                else {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').addClass('text-success');
                }
            };
            return false;
        }

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

		function checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) {
            var hardCutoffTime = 6;
            var currentDateTime = new Date();//can simulate it being other dates and times by changing this value
            console.log("Current datetime returned: " + currentDateTime);
            var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();

            console.log("Hours: " + hours);
            console.log("Day: " + dayOfWeek);

            

            var dateInterval = setInterval(function () {
                var $shipDt = $('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]');

                if ($shipDt.length) {
                    clearInterval(dateInterval);
                    
                    if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
                        //day is saturday, add 2 days and return new date
                        var newDate = addDays(2);
						//var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                        console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
						//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
						viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
						shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
						//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                        //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
						//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                        //return;
                    }

                    if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
                        //cutoff time reached, change date as follows
                        if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
                            //add 3 days making Monday the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(3);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }

                        else {
                            //add 1 day to the date making tomorrow the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(1);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
            

            

        }

        function addDays(days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setDate(date.getDate() + days);
			
			console
            return date;
        }
		
		function checkAndSetShipDateTest(viewModel)
		{
			debugger;
			var hardCutoffTime = 16;
			var currentDateTime = new Date();
			var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();
			
			if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
				var finalDate = addDays(2);
				console.log("New date" + finalDate);
				var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
				var day = finalDate.getDate();
				var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
				console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
				//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
				var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
				viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
				shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
			}
			
			if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
				if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
					var finalDate = addDays(3);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
				else{
					var finalDate = addDays(1);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);

					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);

		}

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

        this.vm.overrideOptimization = false;
        this.vm.arriveByDate = '';
        $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').removeClass('text-success');
		
        client.shipping.loadValue.focus();
        client.shipping.maintabfocus('General');
        client.shipping.subtabfocus('Consignee', 'Account/Tax');

		

        //check and set the CPD checkbox here
        checkAndSetCPD(this.vm);


        //check for CPD flag here, set checked if true
        function checkAndSetCPD(viewModel) {
            //create interval here to watch for CPD checkbox
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $cpdCB = $('[ng-model="vm.cpdProcessFlow"]');

                if ($cpdCB.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    var cpdFlag = sessionStorage.getItem("cpdflag");
                    //status can be True, False or Null

                    if (cpdFlag == "true") {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = true;
                    }
                    else {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = false;
                    }


                }
            }, 10)

        }

		
    }

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
    this.AddPackage = function (shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        this.vm.getWeight();

        if (this.vm.cpdProcessFlow) {
            //$(client.shipping.shipperReference).focus().select();
            $(client.shipping.miscRef7).focus().select();
        }
        else {
            client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
        }
    }

// this.PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns undefined
    this.PostShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {

        //Set the CPD flag to whatever state the this.vm.CPDWorkflow state is
        sessionStorage.setItem("cpdflag", this.vm.cpdProcessFlow);
    }

// GetShipToAddressCustomData() // returns CustomData from the first address book entry
this.GetShipToAddressCustomData = function(){
        //debugger;
        var payloadShipToAddress = {
            "Skip": 0,
            "Take": 10,
            "WhereClauses": [{
                "FieldName": "Id",
                "FieldValue": consigneeId,
                "Operator": 0
            }]
        };
        
        var data = {
            CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
            addressBookIds: addrsBookId,
            SearchCriteria: payloadShipToAddress
        };
        //console.log(data);
      
        ShipToAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', data, false).responseJSON;
    
        console.log(ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[0].CustomData);
        
        return ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[0].CustomData;
                
    };

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
        debugger;
        const st_company = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company.toUpperCase();
        addrsBookId = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.AddressBookId;
        consigneeId = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Id;
        
        if(st_company == "UPS MI" || st_company.includes("MAIL INNOVATIONS"))
        {
            console.log("Mail Innovatoins Shipment");
            console.log(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.AddressBook);
            console.log(addrsBookId);
            console.log(consigneeId);
                
            addressCustomData = this.GetShipToAddressCustomData();
            mi_flag = client.getValueByKey('Custom1',addressCustomData);
                  
            if(mi_flag !== "MI_TPB"){
               throw new Error("Please contact GAP ShipExec Admin for Mail Innovation Authorization [Ship-Exec-stores-dg@gap.com].");
            }
            else
            {
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {
                    Company : "UPS Mail Innovations",
                    Contact : "Shipping",
                    Address1 : "13050 Marlay Ave",
                    Address2 : "Suite 100",
                    City : "Fontana",
                    StateProvince : "CA",
                    PostalCode : "92337",
                    Country : "US",
                    Email : "upsusmi01transportation@ups.com",
                    Account : "7500YW"
                };
                      
            }
        }

        if (pooler)
        {
            if (document.getElementById("pooler").checked)
            {
                for (var p of shipmentRequest.Packages)
                {
                    p.MiscReference4 = vm.profile.Shippers[0].Email.replace("@", "").replace(" ", "").replace(".pool", "").replace(".POOL", "").toUpperCase();
                }               
            }
        }

        var misc3reference = "200.30.6035.5102.90059";
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = "";
            //Address 1
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "1112 Turkey Mountain Rd.")
            {
                console.log('found 1/4 address');
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
            }
             //Address 2
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "102R Demi Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
              //Address 3
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "17511 S. Susana Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
               //Address 4
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "200 Terminal St.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
        }
        console.log('PRESHIP');
        console.log(shipmentRequest);

    };

// Source: GAP INC (GAPMailrooms)_DirectToMobileCBR_1918.cs
// function ConfigureD2MShipment(calleeMethod) // returns undefined
function ConfigureD2MShipment(calleeMethod){
        
        debugger;
        		
		LogStartMethod("ConfigureD2MShipment()",calleeMethod);
				
		var infoMessage = "D2M shipment ";
		
		if (location.hash === '#!/shipping')		
		{
			if (CurrentShipperIsD2MEnabled() && CurrentUserIsD2MEnabled()) 
			{
				infoMessage += "is ENABLED for current shipper and current user";
				
				var originAddressCompany;
				
				var originAddressLoadedInterval = setInterval(function(){
					originAddressCompany = $('[name="company"]:eq(1)').val();
					if (originAddressCompany!=undefined && originAddressCompany.length)
					{
						EnableReturn();
						clearInterval(originAddressLoadedInterval);	
					}
				},50);
			}
			else
			{
				infoMessage += "is NOT ENABLED for shipper and user";
				var isLoaded;
				var removeD2M = setInterval(function(){
					isLoaded = $('#DirectToMobileShipmentID').is(":checked");
					if (isLoaded!=undefined && (isLoaded === false || isLoaded === false))
					{												
						$('#d2m_checkbox_div_id').remove();						
						DisableReturn();
						clearInterval(removeD2M);	
					}
				},50);
				
				
			}
		}
		else
		{
			infoMessage = "WARNING " + infoMessage + "called outside of shipping action";
		}
		LogMethodInfo(infoMessage);
    }

// function setD2MCheckboxAsChecked() // returns undefined
function setD2MCheckboxAsChecked()
	{
		var checkIsLoadedInterval = setInterval(function(){
								
		var checkIsLoaded =  $('#DirectToMobileShipmentID');
	
		if (checkIsLoaded)
		{
			$('#DirectToMobileShipmentID').prop( "checked", true );
			clearInterval(checkIsLoadedInterval);								
		}
	    },50);
	}

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        
        if (location == '/shipping') this.Shipping();
        else if (location == '/history') this.History();
        else if (location == '/closemanifest') this.CloseManifest();
        else if (location == '/manifestdocuments') this.ManifestDocuments();
        else if (location == '/transmit') this.Transmit();
        else if (location == '/groupmanager') this.GroupManager();
        else if (location == '/managedata') this.ManageData();
    }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {
        translateSelectAddressBookOption();
        this.vm.pickupRequestButtonCaption = client.translateToFrench['Pickup Request'];
        this.vm.translations.ThinClient.CreateAShipment = client.translateToFrench['Create a Shipment'];
        this.vm.translations.ThinClient.Reset = client.translateToFrench['Reset'];
        this.vm.translations.ThinClient.Continue = client.translateToFrench['Continue'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Clear = client.translateToFrench['Clear'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.SelectAction = client.translateToFrench['Select Action'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Add = client.translateToFrench['Add'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Update = client.translateToFrench['Update'];
        this.vm.translations.Common.Today = 'hello'

        function translateSelectAddressBookOption () {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $selectAddressBook = $('form[name="addressForm"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"] option[label="Select address book"]');
                if ($selectAddressBook.length >= 3) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $selectAddressBook.each(function () {
                        if (client.translateToFrench[this.text] !== undefined) {
                            $(this).attr('label', client.translateToFrench[this.text]);
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
        }
    }

                }
            });
        }
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
  this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    try
    {
      //alert = function(){}
      this.vm.getWeight();

    }
    catch (error)
    {
      console.log("Error getting weight")
    }
    if (!shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1)
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Loaded Value " + loadValue + " not found")
    } else
    {
      const Lines = JSON.parse(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1);
      Lines.forEach(line =>
      {
        const fila = document.createElement("tr");
        fila.innerHTML = `
            <td>${line.LineNo}</td>
            <td>${line.ItemNo}</td>
            <td>${line.TotalOrderQuantity}</td>
            <td>${line.SaleUnitOfMeasure}</td>
            <td>${line.SaleUnitPrice}</td>
            <td>${line.ItemDescription}</td>
            <td></td>
            <td>${line.UnitWeight}</td>
            <td></td>
            <td>0</td>
            <td>0</td>
            <td><button class='btn btn-xs btn-success glyphicon glyphicon-plus'></button></td>
            <td hidden>${line.IsKitOrBundle}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.KitDetails ? JSON.stringify(line.KitDetails) : "[]"}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.CountryOfOrigin : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportCurrencyCode : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportTariffCode : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportUnitPrice : ""}</td>
            `;
        if (line.IsKitOrBundle && line.KitDetails == null)
        {
          client.alert.Danger("WARNING: Kit Details are empty when Commodity Set to Kit");
        }
        document.querySelector("#miTabla").appendChild(fila);
      });
      editableTable();

      const buttons = document.querySelectorAll("#miTabla button");
      buttons.forEach(button =>
      {
        button.addEventListener("click", function ()
        {
          const fila = this.parentElement.parentElement;
          AddCommodity(fila, 1, 0);
        });
      });
      const tabla = document.querySelector("#miTabla");
      tabla.classList.remove("hidden");
    }
    console.log(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate)
    var today = new Date();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Day = today.getDate();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Year = today.getFullYear();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Month = today.getMonth() + 1;
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != 'US')
    {
      for (var ii = 0; ii < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; ii++)
      {
        shipmentRequest.Packages[ii].CommercialInvoiceMethod = 1;
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country == 'GB')
        {
            console.log(shipmentRequest.Packages[ii]);
            shipmentRequest.Packages[ii].AdditionalHardcopyDocumentation = false;
        }
      }
      
    }

  }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void

this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {

         var input= $('#textVendorNumber').val();
         //debugger;
         //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1=$('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(input);

 throw new Error("Vendor Code/Number must not be null");

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData2 != null) {
            if( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData2 == "Y") {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee != undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 != undefined) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        $('[address-property-name="Consignee"] button[title="Validate Address"]').click();
                    }
                }, 50);
            }
        }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        if (location == '/') {
            var bmvar = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname + "#!/batchmanager";
            window.location.replace(bmvar);
        }
        
        //<a href="" ng-click="vm.linkToDetails(batch.Info.BatchReference)" class="ng-binding">000046</a>
        
        if (window.location.hash == '#!/batchmanager') {
            var waitForT = setInterval(function () {
            //  $('body').delegate('a[ng-click="vm.linkToDetails(0)"]', 'click', function (e) {
            const alink = $('a[ng-click="vm.linkToDetails(batch.Info.BatchReference)"]:visible');
            if (alink.length > 0)
            {
                $(alink).trigger('click');
                clearInterval(waitForT);
            }
            
                        // $('a[ng-click="vm.linkToDetails(0)"]').trigger('click');
                    // }); //end button delegate
        //}
            }, 250);
        }
        
        if (window.location.hash == '#!/batchdetail') {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                try {
                    $('body').delegate('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]', 'click', function (e) {
                        var waitForTable = setInterval(function () {
                            /* The spanTotalBatchItems element text defaults to a value of 0, need to wait until it changes before we continue. */
                            if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) {
                                var currentDate = new Date();
                                var totalBatchItems = parseInt($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text());

                                /* Once this condition is met, we can remove the rows we don't want. */
                                if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) {
                                    clearInterval(waitForTable);
                                    //console.log('table rows condition met.');
                                    /* Loop the table rows. */
                                    $('#tableBatchDetails tr:gt(0)').each(function (x, y) {
                                        var dueDate = new Date($(this).find('td:eq(1)').text());
                                        if (dueDate < currentDate) {
                                            $(this).remove();
                                        }
                                    }).promise().done(function (e) {
                                        $('#tableBatchDetails').show();
                                        var i = $('#tableBatchDetails tr').length;
                                        $('#spanTotalBatchItems').text(i);
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                        }, 250);
                    });

                    /* Event handler for the 'View Labels' button. */
                    $('body').delegate('#buttonViewCheckedLabels', 'click', function (e) {
                        //prevent the subsequent listeners from firing
                        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                        // console.log("Click");
                        ViewCheckedLabels();
                    }); //end button delegate

                    /* Trigger the click of the 'All' button.  Maybe in the future add an id to the element to make the code a bit more readable. */
                    $('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').trigger('click');
                    
                    if (!$('#HazAlertShipment_panel').is(':visible')) {
	                $('#HazAlertShipment_panel').modal('show');
	                $('#HazAlertShipment_panel').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
	                	$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
	                });
	            }
                }
                catch (err) {
                    console.error(err.message);
                }
            }); //end document.ready
        }
        
        if (window.location.hash == '#!/history') {
        }
        
        $('select[id="reports"]').hide();
        $('ul.navbar-nav a:contains("History")').text('Claim Search');
    }

// ViewCheckedLabels() // returns void
function ViewCheckedLabels() {
        const batchItemArr = [];
        $('#tableBatchDetails').find('input[type=checkbox]:checked').each(function () {
            //debugger;
            console.log("Print");
            var btnPrint = $(this).closest('tr').find('input[type="button"][value="Print"]').first().trigger('click');
            batchItemArr.push($(this).attr('data'))
        });
        var dataObject = {};
        dataObject.Action = "RemoveBatchItem";
        let bLen = batchItemArr.length;
        for (let i = 0; i < bLen; i++) {
            if (i == 0) {
                dataObject.Content = batchItemArr[i];
            } else {
                dataObject.Content += "," + batchItemArr[i];
            }
        }
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(dataObject), UserContext: client.userContext };
        //debugger;
        clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false)
    }

// Source: ICON Clinical Research (PRAInternational)_PRA Intl Business Rules_1574.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        //getUserContext();  // Removed for CBR fix 07202022

        /* Only apply these functions to the shipping page. */
        if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") {
            $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
                $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
            })

            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if ((window.jQuery !== undefined) && ($('select[name=Country]').length > 0)) {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);

                    /* Register the event that fires when a user clicks the 'Reset' button on the main page. */
                    $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.newShipment()"]:eq(0)', 'click', function (e) {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                    });

                    /* Disable the ThirdPartyBilling edit button. */
                    $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);

                    /* For select boxes which are enabled, remove the default country of United States. */
                    $('select[name=Country][disabled!=disabled]').prop('selectedIndex', 0);

                    /* Trying to fix a bug where the Ship From country select element is disabled and set to the wrong country. */
                    /* Enable the element. */
                    $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').prop('disabled', false);

                    /* Hide the End Of Day dropdown menu. */
                    $('ul.nav.navbar-nav li.dropdown:eq(1) > a.dropdown-toggle').hide();

                    /* Change captions for tabs when processing return shipments. */
                    /* Register the event on change. */
                    $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]', 'change', function (e) {
                        var isReturn = $(this).val().length > 0;
                        ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
                        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery = isReturn;
                    });

                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                } /* if ((window.jQuery... */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */

        } /* if (window.location.hash... */
    };

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.IsValid = this.IsValidated;
        this.vm.TemplateInit = this.PageInitialize;
        this.vm.emailNotificationAddress = this.EmailNotificationAddress;
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
        ReturnNameAddressCaption(false);
    };

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns undefined
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };
