// ManifestDocuments() // returns undefined
this.ManifestDocuments = function () {
        testbutton();

        function testbutton() {
            $('body').delegate('#buttonExportCODFile', 'click', function () {
                debugger;
                var shipper = $(this).attr('shipper');
                var carrier = $(this).attr('carrier');
                var historyId = $(this).attr('historyId');
                var historyShipDateYear = $(this).attr('shipDateYear');
                var historyShipDateMonth = $(this).attr('shipDateMonth');
                var historyShipDateDay = $(this).attr('shipDateDay');
                var isSftpChecked = $('#SftprBtnId').prop('checked');
                var isLocalChecked = $('#LocalrBtnId').prop('checked');
                debugger;

                // Send data to user method on the server side
                var usermethodParams = { "action": 1, "usercontext": client.userContext, "shipper": shipper, "historyId": historyId, "historyShipDateYear": historyShipDateYear, "historyShipDateMonth": historyShipDateMonth, "historyShipDateDay": historyShipDateDay, "carrier": carrier, "sftpSelectrdStatus": isSftpChecked, "localSelectrdStatus": isLocalChecked };
                var codFileString;

                var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
                
                clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
                    debugger;                  

                    //****New code 01.24.2022****
                    var jsonString = $("<textarea/>").html(response.Data).text();

                    if (jsonString && isLocalChecked) {                        
                        codFileString = jsonString;

                        var data = new Blob([codFileString], { type: 'text/plain' });

                        var ie = navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE\s([\d.]+)/),
                            ie11 = navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident\/7.0/) && navigator.userAgent.match(/rv:11/),
                            ieEdge = navigator.userAgent.match(/Edge/g),
                            ieVer = (ie ? ie[1] : (ie11 ? 11 : (ieEdge ? 12 : -1)));

                        // set the export file name 
                        var exportFileName = "ShipmentRequest" + historyShipDateYear + historyShipDateMonth + historyShipDateDay + "_1_" + shipper + ".txt"

                        if (ieVer > -1) {
                            window.navigator.msSaveBlob(codFileString, exportFileName);

                        } else {
                            var downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                            downloadLink.download = exportFileName;
                            downloadLink.href = window.URL.createObjectURL(data);
                            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
                            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                            downloadLink.click();
                            document.body.removeChild(link);
                        }
                    }
                });          
            })
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest)
    {	
        var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
        {
            if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]'))) 
            {
            /* Stop the timer. */
            clearInterval(checkExist);
            $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').focus();
            }

        }, 100);
        //Store user name and workstation in shipment misc_reference_5 for logging     
        var user_name = $('a[href="/ShipExecThinClient/Manage"]').text();
        
       // var machine_name = Cookies.get("machinename");
        var machine_name = "";
        var cookie = document.cookie.split(';').filter(function(value) {
        return (value.split('=')[0] === 'machine_name')
            })[0];
        if (cookie != undefined) {
            machine_name === cookie.split('=')[1];
        }

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = "[user_name]" + user_name + "^[machine_name]" + machine_name + "^"

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "IMT";
        //shipmentRequest.packages[0].commodity_class = "CLASS_100";
        
        //CHANGE: 6/22/2020	
        //Don't display Load Box for Batch Edits, only for New Shipments
        //Commented this out as not needed KS 6/14/2021
        // var url = window.location.href;
        // var n = url.indexOf("batch_reference");	
        // if(n == -1)
        // {
        //     $(document).ready(function () {
        //         load_btn_OnClick();
        //     });		
        // }		
        
        //$(document).ready(function () {
        //	load_btn_OnClick();
        //});

       // this.vm.resendShipments = resendShipment;
    }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
     this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams)
    {
        
        var misc_reference_5 = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = misc_reference_5 + "[identifier]" + loadValue.trim() + "^";
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
    
    scrollToService(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
    //#region Get Scale Weight
    // get Weight if button isn't disabled
   // debugger;
    var wgt = 0; 
    if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Amount != null)
    {
         wgt = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Amount;
    }

    if (wgt == 0)
    {
        if (this.vm && this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== undefined) {            
        this.vm.getWeight();
        }
    }   
    //#endregion
}

// WaitForElement(eElement, inputValue, bFocus) // returns Promise<boolean>
      WaitForElement: async (eElement, inputValue, bFocus) =>
      {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) =>
        {
          let i = 0;
          const timer = window.setInterval(() =>
          {
            if ($(eElement).length > 0)
            {
              inputValue ? $(eElement).val(inputValue) : undefined;
              bFocus ? $(eElement).focus().select() : undefined;

              resolve(true);
              window.clearInterval(timer);
            }

            if (i === 9)
            {
              reject(false);
              window.clearInterval(timer);
            }

            i++
          }, 200);
        })
      }

    {
      $('#divAugustaOverlay').show();
      $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();

      /* Make sure the input elements don't show previous entries. */
      $('input[required]').attr('autocomplete', 'off');

      /* Remove all but the Shipping option from the dropdown. */
      /* The other dropdowns are removed via the user profile. */
      $('.nav.navbar-nav:first ul.dropdown-menu').find('li:gt(0)').remove();

      /* Remove the logoff link. */
      $('#btnLogOff').remove();

      $('body').delegate('input[required]', 'keydown', (e) =>
      {
        $('input[required]').each((i, v) => 
        {
          $(v).val().length === 0 ? $(v).addClass('required-invalid') : $(v).removeClass('required-invalid');
        });

        $('input[required]').not('.requred-invalid').length === 0 ? $('.btn-augusta').removeAttr('required') : undefined;
      });
    }
  } //end this.PageLoaded

// thinClientApiRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns nothing
    var thinClientApiRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        $.getJSON('config.json', function (config) {
            var shipExecServiceUrl = config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            var authorizationToken = shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http') ? { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token } : '';
            return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken });
        });
    }

// Source: MarkenLLP (MLLP)_Marken_Phase3_CBR_2501.cs
// this.convertFileInputToBase64(inputId, leg) // returns Promise resolving upload payload object
    this.convertFileInputToBase64 = function (inputId, leg) {
        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {

            var data = {};
            const fileInput = $('#' + inputId);

            // Do not continue if there are no files
            if (!fileInput ||
                fileInput.length === 0 ||
                !fileInput[0].files ||
                fileInput[0].files.length === 0) {
                return;
            }

            // Get basic file info
            var file = fileInput[0].files[0];
            var fileName = file.name;

            // Create reader for reading files
            var reader = new FileReader();
            reader.readAsDataURL(file);
            reader.addEventListener("load", function () {

                // Create and return payload for upload call
                data = {
                    Action: "PaperlessDocUpload",
                    FileName: fileName,
                    encodedString: reader.result.split(',')[1],
                    shipperName: that.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper,
                    leg: leg
                }

                resolve(data);

            }, false);

            reader.addEventListener("error", function (error) {
                reject(error);
            }, false);

        });

    }

// function setUploadDelegates() // returns void
    function setUploadDelegates() {

        setCommodityDelegate();

        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change');
        $('body').undelegate('#chkWorldEase', 'change');


        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click', function (e) {
            //debugger;
            //that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "true";

            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput[0].value = null;
            }
            //debugger;
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";

            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            //debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', '');
            debugger;
            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
                if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                    uploadSuccessLabel.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                    $('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear').click();
                }
                else {
                    that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "true";
                    //debugger;
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 1, e).then(function (ret, e) {
                        //debugger;
                        //that.currentShipment.MiscReference19 = JSON.stringify(ret);
                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#chkWorldEase', 'change', function (e) {
            var uploadGoodsDiv = $('#divUploadGoods');
            if (uploadGoodsDiv
                && uploadGoodsDiv.length
                && uploadGoodsDiv.length === 1
                && e.target) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked) {
                    uploadGoodsDiv[0].classList.add('displayNone');
                }
                else {
                    uploadGoodsDiv[0].classList.remove('displayNone');
                }
            }

        });

    };

// function PassWorldeaseTrackingNumber(docboxtrackingNumber) // returns void
    function PassWorldeaseTrackingNumber(docboxtrackingNumber) {
        debugger;

        var jsonData;

        var dataObject = {
            ConsolidationTrackingNumber: docboxtrackingNumber,
            UserContext: clientService1.userContext
        };

        var payload = JSON.stringify(dataObject);

        debugger;

        var data = {
            Data: payload,
            UserContext: clientService1.userContext
        };

        // Show the spinner
        $("#loadingSpinner").show();

        var ajaxRequest = clientService1.thinclientService1APIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);

        ajaxRequest.done(function (data) {
            jsonData = data.Data;
            $("#loadingSpinner").hide();
            console.log(jsonData);
            setTimeout(function () {
                debugger;
                var dataObj = JSON.parse(jsonData.replaceAll('&quot;', '"'));
                var htmlString = '<div>Total Invoice Amount: '
                    + dataObj.Total
                    + ' '
                    + dataObj.TotalUOM
                    + '<br /><hr />';
                var i = 0, len = dataObj.TrackingNumbers.length;
                for (; i < len; i++) {
                    var currentTracking = dataObj.TrackingNumbers[i];
                    var itemString = currentTracking.TrackingNumber
                    htmlString += itemString + "<br />";
                }
                htmlString += '</div>';
                $('#infoModalLabel').html(htmlString);
                $('#infoModal').modal('show');

            }, 50);
        }).fail(function (xhr, status, error) {
            console.error("Error:", error);
            $("#loadingSpinner").hide();
            alert("Failed to get data.");

        }).always(function () {
            // Hide the spinner regardless of success or failure
            $("#loadingSpinner").hide();
        });
    }

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
         }
 
        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;
        
        
            $(document).ready(function() {
               
             $("#OK").on("click", function() {
            
                 var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if(arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)){
                     var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue); 
                     var selectedStudy= arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                     //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                     
                     var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                     var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                     var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                      shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                      
                     var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                     var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                     var selectedSite= arrayOrders2[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                }
                else
                 {
                     alert("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                     throw new Error("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                 }
        
                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                 GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest);
                
                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
                
            });
        
        });
     
    }

// GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    function GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest) {
       var jsonData;
       var dataObject = {
                    StudyReferenceCode:selectedStudy, 
                    UserContext: client.userContext
                };
 
                var payload = JSON.stringify(dataObject);
                debugger;
                var data = { Data: payload, UserContext: client.userContext };
 
                var ajaxRequest = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);
            
                ajaxRequest.done(function (data) {
 
             jsonData = data.Data;
                console.log(jsonData);
               $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(jsonData);
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper=$('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];

                });
            
    }

// ShowOverlay() // returns void
ShowOverlay: function () {
               if ($('div.overlay').length === 0) {
                  //console.log('div.overlay not found, creating');
                  $('div.body-content').first().append($('<div />').addClass('overlay').css({
                     content: '',
                     position: 'fixed',
                     top: 0,
                     left: 0,
                     width: '100vw',
                     height: '100vh',
                     'background-color': 'rgba(0, 0, 0, .25)',
                     'z-index': 1049
                  })).show();
                  /*
          .overlay {
            content: '';
            display: none;
            position: fixed;
            top: 0;
            left: 0;
            width: 100%;
            height: 100%;
            background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, .25);
            z-index: 1049;
          }
        */
               } else {
                  $('div.overlay').show();
               }
            }

// HideOverlay() // returns void
HideOverlay: function () {

               $('div.overlay').hide();
               $('#divModalLoadShipments').hide();
            }

// FocusOnLoadInput() // returns void

               var loadInput;
               if ($('#inputLoadValue').length > 0) {
                  loadInput = '#inputLoadValue';
               } else {
                  loadInput = 'input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]';
               }
               this.WaitForElement(loadInput, undefined, undefined, true);
            }

// function SetShipperAddressAsReturnAddress(element) // returns void
function SetShipperAddressAsReturnAddress(element)
    {
        debugger;
        
        var selectedShipper = "";
        
        if (typeof(element)==="object")
        {
            selectedShipper = $(element).find(":selected").text();
        }
        else if (typeof(element)==="string")
        {
            selectedShipper = element;
        }
        
        var cleanShipper = selectedShipper.replace("string:", "").replace("_", " ");
        
        if (cleanShipper != "" && cleanShipper != undefined )
        {
            
            if(cleanShipper =='16A4Y8 McLane')
            {
                $("#ddlShippingCharge").val("CustomerOrVendor");
            }
            else
            {
             $("#ddlShippingCharge").val("");   
            }
            
            SetShippingCharges(cleanShipper);
            
            var userMethodParams = { "action": "SetShipperAddressAsReturnAddress", "SelectedShipper": cleanShipper};
            
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
            
            var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
            
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } 
            else {
                    var json = DecodeReturnString(response.Data);
                    $('[name="company"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Company);
                    $('[name="contact"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Contact);
                    $('[name="address1"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Address1);
                    $('[name="address2"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Address2);
                    $('[name="address3"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Address3);
                    $('[name="city"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.City);
                    $('[name="stateProvince"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.StateProvince);
                    $('[name="postalCode"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.PostalCode);
                    $('[name="country"]:eq(1)').val(json.Address.Country);
                    vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = json.Address;
                }
        }
        
    }

// function setFocus(element) // returns void
function setFocus(element){
    	var ng = angular.element(element);
    	if (ng.length>0)
    	{
    		ng.focus();
    	}
    }

// function SetUserData(shipmentRequest, isOptimalAccepted) // returns shipmentRequest
function SetUserData(shipmentRequest,isOptimalAccepted = false)
    {
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = $("#ddlShippingCharge").val();
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData2 = $("#ddlIsTobaccoShipment").val();
         var $loadValue = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');
         if ($loadValue.length) {
             shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData3 = $loadValue.val();
         }
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData4 = isOptimalAccepted;
         return shipmentRequest;
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
this.Shipping = function() {
    updateDryIceRegulationSet();
    function updateDryIceRegulationSet() {
        debugger;
        $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.hazmatdryIceBtn"]', 'click', function() {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $dryIceRegulationSet = $('[ng-model="vm.dryIceInfo.DryIceRegulationSet"]');
                if ($dryIceRegulationSet.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $dryIceRegulationSet.find('option[label="Regulations Not Specified"]').remove();
                }
            }, 50);
        });
    }
};

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        this.vm.NotificationAddressEmail = this.AddEmailToNotification;

        originCustomData = getCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);
        if (originCustomData.length) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = getKeyValue('Custom3', originCustomData);
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Contact;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = getKeyValue('Custom2', originCustomData);
        }

        $('body').delegate('div[ng-if="vm.rateResults.length > 0"] tr td a', 'click', serviceUpgrade);

        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();
        if(getUserName() == 'SRPBulletin@mskcc.org' || this.vm.profile.Name == 'FIFTYTHIRDSTREET_Profile'){
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();
        }

        var interval = setInterval(function() {
            var shipperReference = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]')
            var miscReference3 = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference3"]')

            var loaded = shipperReference.length && miscReference3.length;
            if (loaded){
                clearInterval(interval);
                if (getKeyValue('custom5', originCustomData) == 1) {
                    // disable shipper reference on general and reference tab
                    $('div[property="ShipperReference"] input').prop('disabled', true);
                }
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.isMobile = isMobile;
        this.vm.metaBase64 = client.meta.imageBase64;
        this.vm.confirmationMessage = 'We have received your request and will ship boxes out to you soon.  Please check your personal email for shipping confirmation.'
        this.vm.clearNameAddress = clearNameAddress;
        //update fieldoption stateprovince validationdropdown for custom list
        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.StateProvince'].ValidationType = 5;
        this.vm.updateConsigneeStateProvince = updateConsigneeStateProvince;
        this.vm.focusNext = focusNext;
        this.vm.onChangeAssetType = onChangeAssetType;        
        this.vm.addReturnItem = addReturnItem;        
        this.vm.clickedPage = clickedPage;
        this.vm.buildPage = buildPage;
        this.vm.removeReturnItem = removeReturnItem;
        this.vm.returnInstructions = [
            'Please use the below drop-down menu to select the return package and input Meta Asset Tag number or Device Serial Number. For Prototype device, please select the best fit dimension package.',
            'Please only pack one item per package.'
        ]

        function isMobile () {
            var regex_mobile = new RegExp(/Android|BlackBerry|iPhone|iPad|iPod|Opera Mini|IEMobile/, 'i');
            var userAgent = window.navigator.userAgent;
            return regex_mobile.test(userAgent)
        };  

        function buildPage () {
            this.dataWithPagination = [];
            var start = (this.pagination.currentPage-1)*this.pagination.itemsPerPage;
            var end = start + this.pagination.itemsPerPage;
            for (var i = start; i < end; i++) {
                var item = this.dataArray[i];
                if (item != undefined) {
                    this.dataWithPagination.push(item);
                }
            }            
        }

        function clickedPage(e) {
            if (e.target.classList.contains('active')) return;
            this.pagination.currentPage = parseInt(e.target.innerText);
            this.buildPage();
        }        

        function removeReturnItem(index){
            this.dataWithPagination.splice(index, 1);

            var pageIndex = this.pagination.currentPage - 1;
            var pageDataArrayIndex = pageIndex*this.pagination.itemsPerPage;
            this.dataArray.splice(pageDataArrayIndex + index, 1);

            if (this.dataWithPagination.length == 0) {
                this.pagination.currentPage = pageIndex;
            }

            this.pagination.numberOfItems = this.dataArray.length;
            this.pagination.numberOfPages = Math.ceil(this.pagination.numberOfItems/this.pagination.itemsPerPage);
            this.buildPage();            
        }

        function addReturnItem () {            
            var item = {
                AssetType: this.selectedAssetType, 
                BoxSize: this.selectedBoxSize, 
                AssetTagOrSerialNumber: this.assetTagOrSerialNumber
            }
            if (!isComplete(item)) return;
            this.dataArray.push(item);
            this.pagination.numberOfItems = this.dataArray.length;

            var pageCount = Math.ceil(this.pagination.numberOfItems/this.pagination.itemsPerPage);
            if (this.pagination.numberOfPages != pageCount) {
                this.pagination.numberOfPages = pageCount;
                this.pagination.currentPage = pageCount;
                this.dataWithPagination = [];
            }
            
            if (this.dataWithPagination.length == this.pagination.itemsPerPage) {
                this.pagination.currentPage = this.pagination.numberOfPages;
                this.buildPage(); 
            } else {
                this.dataWithPagination.push(item);
            }
            this.clearSelectedReturns();
            $('[ng-model="vm.selectedAssetType"]').focus();
        }

        function focusNext () {
            var activeNgModel = document.activeElement.attributes['ng-model'].value;
            var textArray = $('[type="text"]');
            for (var i = 0; i < textArray.length - 1; i++) {
                var ngModel = textArray[i].attributes['ng-model'].value;
                if (ngModel == activeNgModel) {                    
                    textArray[i+1].focus();
                    return;
                }
            }
            $('button[name="addReturnItem"]').focus();
        }
        
        function onChangeAssetType () {
            var selectedBoxId = this.selectedAssetType.BoxSizeId;
            var boxIndex = $.map(this.boxSize, function(box, index){
                if (box.Id == selectedBoxId) { return index;}
            });
            this.selectedBoxSize = this.boxSize[boxIndex];
         
            this.assetTagOrSerialNumber = this.selectedAssetType.Code == 'LD' ? 'N/A' : '';
            this.readonlyAssetTagOrSerialNumber = this.selectedAssetType.Code == 'LD';

            var returnItem = { AssetType: this.selectedAssetType, BoxSize: this.selectedBoxSize, AssetTagOrSerialNumber: this.assetTagOrSerialNumber };
            isComplete(returnItem);
        }

        function isComplete(item) {
            var result = false;
            if (item.AssetType == '' || item.AssetType.BoxSizeId == 999)
                $('[ng-model="vm.selectedAssetType"]').focus();
            else if (item.BoxSize == '' || item.BoxSize == undefined)
                '[ng-model="vm.selectedBoxSize"]'.focus(); //wait to focus
            else if (item.AssetTagOrSerialNumber == '') {
                $('[ng-model="vm.assetTagOrSerialNumber"]').focus();
            }                
            else 
                result = true;
            return result;
        }
        
        function updateConsigneeStateProvince(country) {
            this.consigneeStateProvince = [];
            if (country == 'US') this.consigneeStateProvince = client.shipping.stateProvince.unitedStates;
            else if (country == 'CA') this.consigneeStateProvince = client.shipping.stateProvince.canada;
            this.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.Phone'].IsRequired = country == 'CA';
        }

        function clearNameAddress(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) {
            if (nameAddress == 'Consignee') {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {
                    Company: this.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.Company'].DefaultValue,
                    Email: client.userName
                }
                shipmentRequest.Packages[this.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = '';
            }
            client.shipping.contact.focus();
        }
    }

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        var userData1 = {};
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.dataArray.length; i++) {
            var item = this.vm.dataArray[i];
            userData1[i + '-AssetCode'] = item.AssetType.Code;
            userData1[i + '-AssetName'] = item.AssetType.Name;
            userData1[i + '-AssetTagOrSerialNumber'] = item.AssetTagOrSerialNumber;
            userData1[i + '-BoxName'] = item.BoxSize.Name;
            userData1[i + '-Length'] = item.BoxSize.Length;
            userData1[i + '-Width'] = item.BoxSize.Width;
            userData1[i + '-Height'] = item.BoxSize.Height;
            userData1[i + '-OutboundWeight'] = item.BoxSize.OutboundWeight;
            userData1[i + '-InboundWeight'] = item.BoxSize.InboundWeight;
        }

        var isOriginSanDiego = client.meta.originSanDiego.includes(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince);
        
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = isOriginSanDiego ? 'UPS_STORE_CA' : 'UPS_STORE_GA';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: 'PLACEHOLDER' };
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = '0';
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].UserData1 = JSON.stringify(userData1);
    }

// PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns undefined
    this.PostShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        if (shipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode == 0) {
            $('#confirmationModal').modal('show');
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        client.shipping.contact.focus();
        
        this.vm.clearSelectedReturns = clearSelectedReturns;
        this.vm.pagination = {
            currentPage: 1,
            itemsPerPage: 6,
            numberOfPages: 1
        };        
        this.vm.tableheight = 40*this.vm.pagination.itemsPerPage+20;
        this.vm.dataArray = [];
        this.vm.dataWithPagination = [];
        this.vm.consigneeStateProvince = [];
        this.vm.selectedReturnItem = '';
        this.vm.returnItemQuantity = '';
        this.vm.readonlyAssetTagOrSerialNumber = false;
        this.vm.returnItems = client.meta.returnItems;
        this.vm.assetType = client.meta.assetType;
        this.vm.boxSize = client.meta.boxSize;
        this.vm.clearSelectedReturns();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {
            Company: this.vm.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.Company'].DefaultValue,
            Email: client.userName
        }
        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = '';

        function clearSelectedReturns() {
            this.selectedAssetType = { BoxSizeId: 999 };
            this.selectedBoxSize = '';
            this.assetTagOrSerialNumber = '';
        }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        appendCSS();
        //getUserContext();  //not used
        //dismissAlertDialog();
        updateDropDownMenu();

        if (location === '/') {
            //document.location = '#!/shipping';

        } else if (location === '/shipping') {
            loadText = angular.element('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');

            $('body').delegate('input[ng-model="nameaddress.StateProvince"]', 'change', function () {
                $(this).val($(this).val().toUpperCase());
            });

            $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Packaging"]', 'change', function () {
                $('#dimensionChange').click();
            });

            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                $consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                consigneeCompany = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');
				consigneePhone = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Phone"]');

                const $generalTab = $('general-tab');
                generalCarrierInstructions = $generalTab.find('[property="CarrierInstructions"]');
                generalDescription = $generalTab.find('[property="Description"]');
                generalAllServices = $generalTab.find('[ng-model="vm.isAllServicesSelected"]').hide();
                generalSpanSelectAll = $generalTab.find('span:contains("Select All")').hide();
                generalDimensionLength = $generalTab.find('[name="length"]');
                generalDimensionWidth = $generalTab.find('[name="width"]');
                generalDimensionHeight = $generalTab.find('[name="height"]');

                $internationalTab = $('international-tab');
                internationalWorldEaseHeading = $internationalTab.find('h5:contains("World Ease")');

                // var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && generalCarrierInstructions.length && generalDescription.length &&
                // generalAllServices.length && generalSpanSelectAll.length && generalDimensionLength.length && generalDimensionWidth.length && generalDimensionHeight.length;

                // var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && generalCarrierInstructions.length && generalDescription.length &&
                //     generalDimensionLength.length && generalDimensionWidth.length && generalDimensionHeight.length && $accessorialsTab.length;

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && generalDescription.length && internationalWorldEaseHeading.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    //debugger;
                    pageLoaded = true;
                    documentReady();
                }
            }, 100);

            setFocus(loadText);
        }
    };

// appendDownloadMenu() // returns void
    function appendDownloadMenu () {
        $('body').on('click', '#sws-menu-item', function(e) {
            $('#StrattonWarrenFileDownload').click();
        })
        
        downloadMenu = true;
        var html = [
            '<li class="dropdown">',
                '<a class="dropdown-toggle" data-toggle="dropdown" href="">Downloads<span class="caret"></span></a>',
                '<ul class="dropdown-menu">',
                    '<li id="sws-menu-item"><a>Stratton Warren File</a></li>',
                    '<li role="separator" class="divider"></li>',
                    '<li id="gl-menu-item"><a href="javascript:glCodeFileDownload()">GL Code File</a></li>',
                '</ul>',
            '</li>',
            '<li id="download-loading">',
                '<img src="/Content/img/spinner-transparent.gif" class="loading-spinner" />',
                '<span class="loading-text"> Loading...</span>',
            '</li>'
        ].join("\n");

        //$('div > div.navbar.navbar-default.navbar-fixed-top > div > div.navbar-collapse.collapse > ul').append(html);
        $('div > div.navbar.navbar-default.navbar-fixed-top > div > div.navbar-collapse.collapse > div > ul').append(html);
    }

// toggleDownloadLoading(downloading, menuOption) // returns void
    function toggleDownloadLoading(downloading, menuOption) {
        let menuItem = "";

        $('#download-loading').toggle();
        
        switch (menuOption) {
            case "SWS" : menuItem = "#sws-menu-item"; break;
            case "GLCODE" : menuItem = "#gl-menu-item"; break;
        }
        $(menuItem).toggleClass('disabled', downloading);
    }

// GLCodeUserMethod(e) // returns void
    this.GLCodeUserMethod = function (e) {
        //debugger;
        let option = "GLCODE";
        let data = { Action: option, Content: ''};
        let title = "GL Code File Download";
        let thisRef = this;

        // show loading spinner
        toggleDownloadLoading(true, option);
        
       $.post({
            url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'json',
			headers: clientService.authorizationToken(),
            data: Object.assign({ UserContext: client.userContext }, { Data: JSON.stringify(data) })
        }).done(function(response) {
            showModalDialog(thisRef, title, response, option);
        }).fail(function(error) {
            showModalDialog(thisRef, title, error.responseText, option);
        });
    }

// StrattonWarrenUserMethod(e) // returns void
    this.StrattonWarrenUserMethod = function (e) {
        // debugger;
        let option = "SWS";
        let data = { Action: option, Content: ''};
        let title = "Stratton Warren File Download";
        let thisRef = this;

        // show loading spinner
        toggleDownloadLoading(true, option);
        
        $.post({
            url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'json',
			headers: clientService.authorizationToken(),
            data: Object.assign({ UserContext: client.userContext }, { Data: JSON.stringify(data) })
        }).done(function(response) {
            showModalDialog(thisRef, title, response, option);
        }).fail(function(error) {
            showModalDialog(thisRef, title, error.responseText, option);
        });
    }

// showModalDialog(thisRef, title, response, option) // returns void
    function showModalDialog(thisRef, title, response, option) {
        //debugger;
        // hide loading spinner
        toggleDownloadLoading(false, option);
        decodeReturnString(response);

        thisRef.AlertTitle = title;
        if (response.ErrorCode == 0) {
            thisRef.AlertMessage = response.Data;
        } else {
            thisRef.AlertMessage = response.ErrorMessage;
        }
        // setting dom values since ng-model isn't available
        var responseText = response.ErrorCode == 0 || !response.ErrorMessage  ? response.Data : response.ErrorMessage
        alertModal.find('h4').text(title);
        alertModal.find('p').text(responseText);
        alertModal.modal('show');
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined

// Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {

        //uncomment this to auto get weight
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
        debugger;

        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }//end of this.shipping

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {

        //enable this to get weight auto at order load time
        this.vm.getWeight();
		debugger;
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
        checkForCancelled(this.vm);
        sumCommodities();

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

        function checkForCancelled(view) {

            var $misc19 = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]');

            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if ($misc19.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);

                        if ($misc19.val() == "T") {
                            debugger;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip = true;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisablePendingShipment = true;
                            $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            alert("This order is marked as Cancelled. Please load a new order");
                        }
                    }
                }, 50);

            }
        }
		

        function sumCommodities()
        {
            var commoditiesValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents.map(m => +m.Quantity * +m.UnitValue.Amount);
            var commTotal = 0.00;
            if(!commoditiesValue || Array.isArray(commoditiesValue ) || arr.commoditiesValue  !== 0)
            {
                for (let i = 0; i < commoditiesValue.length; i++) {
                    commTotal += commoditiesValue[i];
                  }
            }
            $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $' + commTotal);
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').removeClass('text-success');

        $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $');
		
        client.shipping.loadValue.focus();
        client.shipping.maintabfocus('General');
        client.shipping.subtabfocus('Consignee', 'Account/Tax');

        $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', false);
        $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', false);
        $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', false);
    }

    }

// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// Source: National Collectors Mint (NACOMI)_NCM Trial CBR_2467.cs
// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {
        
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
                loadText = ('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');  
                
                var loaded = loadText.length;
                
                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }, 50);
            
        appendCSS();

        this.vm.loadWeight = loadWeight;
        
        function loadWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration === undefined) return;
            var scale = this.profile.ScaleConfiguration;
            var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read';
            var data = {
                'PortType': scale.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                'Port': scale.Port,
                'UsbVid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                'UsbPid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                'RequestCommand': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                'BaudRate': scale.ScaleDefinition.BaudRate,
                'StopBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                'Parity': scale.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                'DataBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.DataBits,
                'RequestTimeout': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                'HostAddress': scale.HostAddress,
                'RegexPattern': scale.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                'DeviceParser': scale.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                'DeviceName': scale.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                'Handshake': scale.ScaleDefinition.Handshake,
                'RetryCount': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryCount,
                'RetryDelay': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryDelay
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": ret.WeightUnit === null ? "LB" : ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                };


            } else {
                client.alert.Danger(this.translations.Common.ErrorCode + " : " + ret.ErrorCode + "  " + ret.ErrorMessage);
            }            
        }
    }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        this.vm.loadWeight();
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        if (location === '/shipping')
        {
            var loadInterval = setInterval(function()
            {
                loadText = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');
                if (loadText.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(loadInterval);
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }, 50);
            $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]', 'keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.keyCode == 13 && $(this).val().indexOf(".") !== -1)
                {
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[1]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[2]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[0]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                }
            });
        }
    };

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        //Setting the return address on Dicks Sporting Goods orders to their address
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 == "8778469997")
        {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Company = "Dicks Sporting Goods";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Contact = "";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Address1 = "1314 Conklin Rd.";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Address2 = "STE B";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.City = "Conklin";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.StateProvince = "NY";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.PostalCode = "13748";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Country = "US";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Phone = "8778469997";
        }
        
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling)
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = addressBookEntries[0].Company;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Contact = addressBookEntries[0].Contact;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = addressBookEntries[0].Address1;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = addressBookEntries[0].Address2;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address3 = addressBookEntries[0].Address3;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = addressBookEntries[0].City;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = addressBookEntries[0].StateProvince;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = addressBookEntries[0].PostalCode;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = addressBookEntries[0].Country;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Phone = addressBookEntries[0].Phone;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }   
        else if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms == "CONSIGNEE")
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }
        $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]').focus();
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData4 == "RTGD")
        {
            alert("Please ensure to rate and select the desired service for shipping.");
        }
    };

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
	    vm = this.vm;
	    //console.log(vm);
		globalVar = location;
		if (globalVar === '/createbatch') {
			var checkExist = setInterval(function() {
				if (window.jQuery) {
					/* Stop the timer */
					clearInterval(checkExist);
					var emailText = "";
					var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
					Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag) {
						if (tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!", "").trim();
					});
					let i = emailText.indexOf("@");
					$('input[name="batchReference"]').val(emailText.substring(0, i) + GetDateTimeToString()).change();

				}
			}, 50);
			
			HighlightWrongOrderNumber();
		}
		
		
        if (globalVar === '/scanship') {
        	HighlightWrongOrderNumber();
        }
		
		if (globalVar === '/history' || globalVar === '/groupmanager' ) {
			var emailText = "";
			var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
			Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag) {
				if (tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!", "").trim();
			});
			let i = emailText.indexOf("@");
			if(emailText.substring(0, i)==='demo0')
			{ ReplaceAccountNumberWithXXXXXX();} 
        }
        
        if(globalVar === '/closemanifest'){
            // Provide a default label function to avoid "undefined" in the select
            vm.getManifestLabel = function(item) {
                // Show nothing or a placeholder until real data is loaded
                return item && item.Name ? item.Name : '';
            };
            getDates(vm);
        }
        
	}

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;        
        //$.get({ url: "http://localhost:9091/api/websites/96659", cache: false })
        //    .fail(function (e) {
        //        alert('The Scale Service may not be running. Please check to make sure the ShipExec Client Service is running');
        //    });
        //}
     
        if(scale == 'EC')   {
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: "http://localhost:9093/api/websites/96659",
                async: false,
                cache: false,
                success: function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    //alert(result);
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5= result;
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference7= "EC";                       
                },
                error: function(jqXhr, exception) {
                alert("Please check the Express Cube Scale Service to make sure the service is running " + exception);                    
                }
            });
        }
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount;                        

        if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 !== null)              {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 == 'YES' ) {
                shipmentRequest.AlertTitle = "ShipExec Alert";
                shipmentRequest.AlertMessage = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference + " has previously shipped today " + shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ShipDate +  ". Click Yes to ship again. Click No to abort.";
                angular.element('[ng-model="AlertModal"]').modal('show');
            }
        }
        
        if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 !== null)              {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 !== 'ADDRESS1MATCH' ) {
                //alert("The Address Line 1 was not matched. Please run Address Validation prior to shipping this package");
                this.vm.alerts = [{type:'danger', msg:'The Address Line 1 was not matched. Please run Address Validation prior to shipping this package'}];
            }   
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;        
        shipmentRequest.AlertTitle = '';
        shipmentRequest.AlertMessage = '';
        angular.element('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').focus();
        
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper="OEMCONNECT";
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms="SHIPPER";
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging="CUSTOM";
        //var Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.GND", Name: "UPS Ground (CSAdapter)" };
        var Service = { Symbol: "OEMCONNE.Custom.SPPS", Name: "UPS SurePost lb or Greater" };        
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = Service;
        var ConsigneeAddress = {Country: "US"};
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = ConsigneeAddress;  
    }

                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference7= "EC";

                }
            });
        }	    
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function(location){
        if(location =="/shipping"){
            // $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] input[name="PostalCode"]', 'keydown', function() {
            //    alert('hello');
            //});
            
            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="ThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'change', function() {
                var $thirdPartyBilling = $('name-address[address-property-name="ThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]');
                if($thirdPartyBilling.val() != "string:--------------------"){
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="ThirdPartyBillingAddress"] button[title="Search Addresses"]').click();
                    //alert($thirdPartyBilling.val());
                } 
            })
            
            var startTime = new Date();
            var pageLoaded = setInterval(function() {
                if ((new Date().getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000 >= 2) {
                    clearInterval(pageLoaded);
                    console.log('clearinterval')
                } else {
                    var tpbFound = false;
                    var consigneeFound = false;
                    var $thirdPartyBillingAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="ThirdPartyBillingAddress"]');
                    var tpbSearchAddress = $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]');
                    var $consignee = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                    var consineeSearchAddress = $consignee.find('[title="Search Addresses"]');
                    if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.length && tpbSearchAddress.length) {
                        tpbFound = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($consignee.length && consineeSearchAddress.length) {
                        consigneeFound = true;
                    }
                    var loaded = tpbFound && consigneeFound;
                    

                    console.log(`is consignee loaded: ${loaded}`)

                    if (loaded) {
                        if($thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').length > 0){
                            startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);

                    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
       
        /* Only apply these functions to the shipping page. */
        if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") {
            $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
                $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
            })

            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if ((window.jQuery !== undefined) && ($('select[name=Country]').length > 0)) {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);

                    /* Register the event that fires when a user clicks the 'Reset' button on the main page. */
                    $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.newShipment()"]:eq(0)', 'click', function (e) {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                    });

                    /* Disable the ThirdPartyBilling edit button. */
                    $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);

                    /* For select boxes which are enabled, remove the default country of United States. */
                    $('select[name=Country][disabled!=disabled]').prop('selectedIndex', 0);

                    /* Trying to fix a bug where the Ship From country select element is disabled and set to the wrong country. */
                    /* Enable the element. */
                    $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').prop('disabled', false);

                    /* Hide the End Of Day dropdown menu. */
                    $('ul.nav.navbar-nav li.dropdown:eq(1) > a.dropdown-toggle').hide();

                    /* Change captions for tabs when processing return shipments. */
                    /* Register the event on change. */
                    $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]', 'change', function (e) {
                        var isReturn = $(this).val().length > 0;
                        ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
                        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery = isReturn;
                    });

                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                } /* if ((window.jQuery... */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */

        } /* if (window.location.hash... */
    };

// checkOriginConsigneeCountry() // returns boolean|void
function checkOriginConsigneeCountry() {
        var shipFromCountry = getObjectValue(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country);
        var shipToCountry = getObjectValue(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country);

        /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
        if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
            DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
            return false;
        }

        if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
            /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
            SetThirdPartyBilling(vm.currentShipment);
        }
        else {
            /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
            if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                SetThirdPartyBilling(vm.currentShipment);
            }

            //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
        }

        if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
        }
    }

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns void|boolean
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };

// SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) // returns void
function SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) {
        /* This enables the button to edit the Third Party Billing Information. */
        $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', false).attr('disabled', false);

        /* Check the box for Third Party Billing which will bring up the modal.  Fill the modal with values.  Click Save. */
        $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('checked', true).attr('checked', true).change();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {}
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = 'PRA Global';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = '995 Research Park Blvd';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = 'Suite 300';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = 'Charlottesville';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = 'VA';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = '22911';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = '883F79';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = 'US'
    }

// DisableThirdPartyBillingElements() // returns void
function DisableThirdPartyBillingElements() {
        $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('checked', false).attr('checked', false);
        $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);
    }

// HidingDefaultShipDate() // returns undefined
function HidingDefaultShipDate () {
        var date = new Date();
        var dateStr = date.getFullYear() + "-" + ("00" + (date.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "-" + ("00" + date.getDate()).slice(-2);
        //debugger;
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var input = $('input[datepicker-options="vm.shipDateOptions"]');
            if (input.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                input.value(dateStr);
            }
        }, 50);
        
        
        
    }

// thinClientApiRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns jqXHR
var thinClientApiRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        $.getJSON('config.json', function (config) {
            var shipExecServiceUrl = config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            var authorizationToken = shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http') ? { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token } : '';
            return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken });
        });
    }

// CopyShipperList() // returns void
function CopyShipperList() {
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
        debugger;
        let shipper = $('shipper-carrier');
            if (shipper.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                let div1 = shipper.find('div');
                let div2 = div1.find('div');
                let div3 = div2.find('div');
                let dpShip = div3.find('Select[ng-model="vm.selectedShipper"]');
                let dpOpt = dpShip.find('option');
                var $options = dpOpt.clone();
                $('#gateway').append($options);
            }
        }, 50);
        
        
    }

this.PageLoaded = function(location) {

// function getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// function getUserContext() // returns void
function getUserContext() {
        debugger;
        if (userContext === undefined) {
            $.get({ url: "api/usercontext/GET", async:false })
            .done(function (data) {
               userContext = data;
            })
        }
    }

// toggleDownloadLoading(downloading) // returns undefined
    function toggleDownloadLoading(downloading) {
