    }

// PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //debugger;
        //getWeight(this.vm);   // TODO: disabled until scale issue resolved
		
		// signed checkbox value
		let signedChecked = $('.form-check[property=MiscReference19]').find('input').prop('checked');
		if (signedChecked === true) {
			userParams.autoship = "autoship";
		}
    };

// PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === undefined) {
			alert("No service selected!");
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null  && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage === 'validate')
		{
			// click validate button
			$('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('button[ng-click="validate(nameaddress)"]').click();
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(0, 4) === 'pop:') {
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== '')
		{
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}
		
		//getWeight(this.vm);   // TODO: disabled until scale issue resolved
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship')
		{
			if (!this.vm.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip) {
				this.vm.checkShip();
			}
		}
    };

// downloadFromCin7API() // returns undefined
    this.downloadFromCin7API = function() {
		//debugger;
		let data = { Action: 'Download_Orders', Params: ''};
		
		downloadOrders = true;
		toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);

		// call SBR UserMethod to access Cin7 API to download orders
		$.post({
			url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
			headers: clientService.authorizationToken(),
			data: {
			    UserContext: client.userContext,
			    Data: JSON.stringify(data)
			}
		}).done(function (data) {
		    //debugger;
			downloadOrders = false;
		    toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);
		    
			if (data.Data === true) {
				alert('Download successful!');
			}
			else {
				alert('Download was not successful');
			}
		}).fail(function (err) {
		    //debugger;
			downloadOrders = false;
		    toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);
			console.log(err.responseJSON);
			alert('Download was not successful');
		});
	}

            this.vm.profile.Shippers = shippers.sort(function (a, b) {

        }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {
        debugger;
        this.vm.keyDown = keyDown;

        $('body').keydown(this.vm, function (event) {
            event.data.keyDownAction = undefined;
            if (event.key === "/") {

                $('#cbrKeydown').click();
            }
        });

            this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Contact = "hello";
            this.selectedServices = [
                { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.NDS" }
            ];
        }           
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {

                var selectAll = $('input[ng-model="vm.isAllServicesSelected"]');

                    clearInterval(checkboxInterval); // <-- important to turn the interval off
                    selectAll.hide();
                    $(".chkLabel").hide();                    
                    $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"]').hide();
                    $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').hide();
                    $('div[ng-if="vm.showServiceSelection"]').attr("class", "col-md-6 no-left-right-padding");
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').on('input', function () {
                        this.value = this.value.match(/^\d+\.?\d{0,2}/);
                    });
                }
            }, 200);
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        // set defaults
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference7 = "No";
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11 = "-- choose option --";
        $('#LoadInput').prop('disabled', false);
        $('#LoadButton').prop('disabled', false);
        $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"]').hide();
        $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').hide();
        
        // Pending Shipment
        $('body').on('click', 'table[aria-describedby="Pending Shipments"] input[type="button"]', this.vm, function(e) {
            $("[property=MiscReference12] input").attr('maxlength','35'); // limit the charecter number for the service change reason field
            $('body').delegate('select[property="Service"]', 'change', function (e) { serviceChangeOptions(this.value); });
            $('body').delegate('[property="MiscReference11"] select', 'change', function (e) { serviceChangeComment(this.value); });
            $('#LoadInput').prop('disabled', true);
            $('#LoadButton').prop('disabled', true);
            serviceChangeOptionsPending();
        });
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function()

    {
		
		
        //Set Consignee Countries
        var consigneeCountries = ['', 'US', 'CA', 'AU']
        setConsigneeCountries(consigneeCountries);

        //Set Currency Options
        declaredValueCurrencyOptions();
        customsDeclaredValueCurrencyOptions();
        commodityUnitValueCurrencyOptions();
        invoiceDiscountCurrencyOptions();
        invoiceFreightCurrencyOptions();
        invoiceInsuranceFeeCurrencyOptions();


        $(document).ready(function () {
            filterPickupPaymentType();
        });

        function filterPickupPaymentType() {
            $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.createPickupRequestClick()"]', 'click', function (event) {
                var list = ['PAY_BY_SHIPPER_ACCOUNT'];
                var element = '[ng-model="vm.pickup.PaymentType"] option';
                replaceOptionValues(list, element);
            });
        }
        //var currencies = ['USD', 'CAD'];
        //setCurrency(currencies);
    }

// setConsigneeCountries(selectedCountries) // returns void
    function setConsigneeCountries(selectedCountries)
    {
        var countryStringValue = ('string:' + selectedCountries.join('|string:')).split('|');
        var interval = setInterval(function()

        {
            var consigneeCountries = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"] option');
            if (consigneeCountries.length)
            {
                clearInterval(interval);
                Array.from(consigneeCountries).forEach(function(opt)

                {
                    if (opt.value != '')
                    {
                        if (!countryStringValue.includes(opt.value))
                        {
                            opt.remove();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }, 50);            
    }

// declaredValueCurrencyOptions() // returns void
    function declaredValueCurrencyOptions()
    {
        var list = ['USD', 'CAD'];
        var element = '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueAmount.Currency"] option';
        setCurrencyOptions(list, element);
    }

    }

// setCurrencyOptions(list, element) // returns void
function setCurrencyOptions(list, element)
    {
        var interval = setInterval(function() 
            {
                var currencies = $(element);
                if (currencies.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function(){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
    }

// replaceOptionValues(list, element) // returns void
 function replaceOptionValues(list, element) {
        var valuelist = list.map(function (e) { return 'string:' + e });
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
            var $element = $(element);
            if ($element.length) {
                clearInterval(interval);
                $element.each(function () {
                    if (!valuelist.includes(this.value) && this.value != '') this.remove();
                });
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest)
    {
    this.vm.shipMode = 0;
    this.vm.disableShipMode = true;
    filterPickupPaymentType();

        function filterPickupPaymentType() {
            var list = ['Pay by shipper account'];            
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var currencies = $('[ng-model="vm.pickup.PaymentType"] option');
                if (currencies.length) {
                    debugger;
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function (){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
        }
}

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {

    //debugger;

    //Map Store Number to ShipperReference
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = nameaddress.Code;

    //Set Default Services Based on From and To Countries		
    var fromCountry = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country;
    var toCountry = nameaddress.Country;

    //Email Address Mappings
	if(nameaddress.Email != null)
	{
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
	}

    //Store Address Book ID value in MiscReference20 to signify that consignee address came from Address Book and was not manually entered.
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = nameaddress.AddressBookId.toString();


    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.GND")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}
}

// SetSelectedService(serviceSymbol) // returns void
this.SetSelectedService = function(serviceSymbol)
    {
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.Services.length; i++)
        {
            if (this.vm.profile.Services[i].Symbol === serviceSymbol)
            {
                this.vm.selectedServices = [this.vm.profile.Services[i]];
                this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = this.vm.profile.Services[i];
                break;
            }
        }
    }
}

// SetCurrencyCAD(shipToCountry) // returns void
this.SetCurrencyCAD = function(shipToCountry)
{
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        if (shipToCountry === "CA")
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
        }
        else
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "USD" };
        }
    }
}

// Source: Sazerac (Sazerac)_Sazerac CBR_1680.cs
// openFileDialog() // returns undefined
function openFileDialog() {
        //debugger;
        var filesSelected = document.getElementById("fileLoader");

        if (filesSelected !== undefined) {
            const fileReader = new FileReader();

            if (filesSelected.files[0]) {
                fileReader.readAsDataURL(filesSelected.files[0]);
            }

            fileReader.onload = function (event) {
                var files = event.target.result;

                // Get base64 file data
                var contents = event.target.result.split(',')[1];

                // adding prefix to beginning of file data to send to user method
                var fileData = "file|" + contents;

                // $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
                // {
                //     UserContext: userContext,
                //     Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)

                // updated for 2.3
                $.post({
                    url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                    data: {
                        UserContext: client.userContext,
                        Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)
                    },
                    headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                }).done(function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    // result.Data should be unencoded [Success] or [Error] string
                    if (result.ErrorCode === 0 && result.Data !== undefined && result.Data.indexOf('[Error]') == -1) {
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                    else {
                        // display error
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                }).fail(function (e) {
                    alert(e.message);
                });
            };
        }
    }

// decodeReturnString(data) // returns parsed data object or undefined on error
function decodeReturnString(data) {
        try {
            data.Data = JSON.parse($('<div />').html(data.Data).text());
            if (data.ErrorMessage) {
                data.ErrorMessage = $('<div />').html(data.ErrorMessage).text();
            }
            return data;
        }
        catch (error) {
            console.log(error);
            //console.log(data);
        }
    }

// ParseJson(result) // returns undefined
function ParseJson(result) {
        //debugger;
        var jsonLoad = result; //jQuery.parseJSON(result);
       
        if (jsonLoad !== null && jsonLoad !== undefined)
        {
            $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
    
            //#region Build Drop-Down List
            var html = "";

            for (let i in jsonLoad.listData)
            {
                html += "<option value='" + jsonLoad.listData[i].glCode + "'>" + jsonLoad.listData[i].fullName + " " + jsonLoad.listData[i].glCode + "</option>";
            }
    
            if (jsonLoad.listData.length === 0)
            {
                alert("No records were returned from search")
            }
            else //More than one record returned
            {
                //$("#costcodes").remove();
                //$(html).insertAfter("#searchButton");
                $("#costcodes").append(html);
                $('#costcodes').change(function() {
                    populateShipExec();
                });
                $("#costcodes").show();
            }
    
        }
        else
        {
            alert("Error populating dropdown box --- " + jsonLoad.ErrorMessage);
        }
    
    }

// populateShipExec() // returns undefined
function populateShipExec() {
        //Get cost code value from selected value in drop down list
        var costcode = document.getElementById('costcodes').value;
        var fullitemtext = document.getElementById('costcodes').options[document.getElementById('costcodes').selectedIndex].text;
    
        //Populate Cost Code in shipper_reference field
        vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].ShipperReference = costcode;
    
        //Populate Full Value in Reference Field 3
        vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference3 = fullitemtext;
    
        //Reset ShipExec Controls
        //document.getElementById('costcodes').outerHTML = "";
        $('#costcodes').off('change');
        $('#costcodes option:not(:first)').remove();
        $('#costcodes').hide();
        ////resetShipExec();
        $('#search_input').val('');
        $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
    }

// resetShipExec() // returns undefined
function resetShipExec() {    
        $('#search_input').val('');
        $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
        $('#ship_goods_type').val("default");
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        vm = this.vm;
        appendCSS();
        dismissAlertDialog();

        if (location === '/shipping') {
            consigneeStateIsRequired = vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired;
            consigneePhoneIsRequired = vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired;
            descriptionIsRequired = vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired;

            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]')
                consigneeState = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');
                consigneeCountry = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="Country"]');
                consigneePhoneLabel = $consigneeNameAddress.find('label:contains("Phone")');
                consigneePhone = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="Phone"]');

                descriptionLabel = $('label:contains("Description Of Goods")');

                var loaded = consigneeCountry.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    pageLoaded = true;
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    documentReady();
                }
            }, 50);
        }
    };

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.IsValid = this.IsValidated;
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);

        if (!this.vm.IsValid('ShipperReference', shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference)) {
            throw ({ message: 'Cost Center is invalid from User Custom Data', errorCode: '001' });
        }

        if (pageLoaded) {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = consigneeStateIsRequired;
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = consigneePhoneIsRequired
            vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = descriptionIsRequired;
        }
    };

// documentReady() // returns void
    function documentReady() {
        vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = false;
        descriptionLabel.css('color', '#333333');

        vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = false;
        consigneePhoneLabel.css('color', '#333333');
        consigneePhone.css('border-color', 'rgb(204,204,204)')

        consigneeCountry.change(function (e) {
            setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement();
        });

    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {

// GetDataManagementContents(apiMethod) // returns void
    this.GetDataManagementContents = function (apiMethod) {
        var userContext = this.GetUserContext();
        var thinClientAPIRequest = this.thinClientAPIRequest;

        var data = { CompanyId: userContext.CompanyId };
        thinClientAPIRequest(apiMethod, data, true).done(function (result) {
            if (result.ErrorCode == 0) {
                var userObject = { Action: apiMethod, Data: JSON.stringify(result) };
                data = { Data: btoa(JSON.stringify(userObject)), UserContext: userContext };
                thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);//.done(function (result) { debugger; });
            };
        });
    }

// thinClientAPIRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns jQuery AJAX promise
    this.thinClientAPIRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = client.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = client.getAuthorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken })
    }

// focus(selector) // returns number
        focus: function (selector) {
            if (setFocus(selector) == 0) {
                var intervalId = setInterval(function () {
                    if (setFocus(selector)) clearInterval(intervalId)
                }, 10)
            }

            function setFocus(selector) {
                var element = $(selector);
                element.focus();
                return element.length;
            }
        }

// thinClientApiRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns undefined
var thinClientApiRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        $.getJSON('config.json', function (config) {
            var shipExecServiceUrl = config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            var authorizationToken = shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http') ? { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token } : '';
            return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken });
        });
    }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) 
    {               
        loadselectedValue=loadValue;
        // Converting JS object to an array
        shipmentRequestObject =  JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
        
        ChromeScrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

        // Check for not found error
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(0,1) == '~')    
                {
                 alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(1));
				  $("input:text").eq(0).focus();   
			  this.vm.newShipment();
	        	return;
                }
        }
        
        //Send OSCO related errors to end user
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if (window.confirm(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20 + "\nContinue with shipment?")) 
            {
              //alert("You pressed OK");
            } 
            else 
            {
                $("input:text").eq(0).focus();
            }   
        }
      
        // Check for address validation required
        if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4 == 'Y')    
                {
                var interval = setInterval(function() {
                const consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                consigneeCompany = consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');
                consigneePostalCode = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="postalCode"]');
                consigneeCity = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                consigneeState = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && consigneePostalCode.length && consigneeCity.length && consigneeState.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] button[title="Validate Address"]').click();                    
                    }
                }, 50);
            }
        }
  
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1);
        
        $('[name="company"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company);
        
    //debugger;
    }

// function ChromeScrollIntoView(element, value) // returns void
    function ChromeScrollIntoView(element, value) {
        if (!isIE()) {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                if (element.val() == value) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
     
                    var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                    var selectTop = element.offset().top;
     
                    element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                }
            }, 50);
        }
    }

// function ClearAllInputFields() // returns void
    function ClearAllInputFields()
    {
        var loadedOrderValue = $('input[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').val();
        var elements = document.getElementsByTagName("input");        
        for (var ii=0; ii < elements.length; ii++) 
        {
            if (elements[ii].type == "text" && elements[ii].value != loadedOrderValue) 
            {
                elements[ii].value = "";
            }
        }  
        
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').prop("checked", false);
        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]>option:eq(0)').prop('selected', true)
        $('textarea[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val();
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val();
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmailLocale"]').val();
         shipmentRequestObject =  {}
    }

    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;
          var employeeID;
          var BU;
          var OU;
          var CR;
          var locationCode;
         var CustomData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
            for (var Custom in CustomData) {
                     if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom1") employeeID = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                      if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom2") BU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                       if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom3") OU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                        if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom4") CR = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                         if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom5")  locationCode= CustomData[Custom].Value;
             }
             
         if (CR === undefined || !isFiveDigitNumber(CR)) {
            alert('Invalid Cost Center');
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = employeeID;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = CR;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = CR;
         shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = BU;
          shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = locationCode;
    }

// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
    function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// getUserContext() // returns void
    function getUserContext() {
        debugger;
        if (userContext === undefined) {
            $.get({ url: "api/usercontext/GET", async:false })
            .done(function (data) {
               userContext = data;
            })
        }
    }

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

        if (!angular.element('input[value="Get Weight"]').prop('disabled')){
            if (vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount == undefined) {
                vm.getWeight();
            }
        }
        var startTime = new Date();
        var weightExists = setInterval(() => {
            if ((new Date().getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000 >= 2) {
                clearInterval(weightExists);
            } else {
                if (vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount != undefined) {
                    startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);
                    vm.checkShip();
                    //$('#myShipBtn').click()
                }
            }
        }, 333);
    }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
    debugger;
    var consolidatedOpportunities = $("#txtConsolidatedFields").find('*').filter(':input:visible:first').val();
    
       if ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked") && ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities))
       {
         var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("true",consolidatedOpportunities,loadValue);
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession;
       }
       else
       {
            var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("false","",loadValue);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession
       }
    }

// ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities) // returns boolean
function ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities)
    {
        var rexVal = /^[A-Z0-9]+((,|-)[A-Z0-9]+)*[A-Z0-9]+$/;
        var result = true;
        if (!rexVal.test(consolidatedOpportunities.toUpperCase()))
        {
            if (consolidatedOpportunities.trim()==="")
            {
                result=true;
            }
            else
            {
                alert("Consolidated opportunities not well formed.");
                result= false;
            }
        }
        return result;
    }

// CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping, ConsolidatedOpportunities, OpportunityLoaded) // returns string
function CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping,ConsolidatedOpportunities,OpportunityLoaded)
    {
        var jsonObject = {};
        jsonObject["IsConsolidatedShipping"] = IsConsolidatedShipping;
        jsonObject["ConsolidatedOpportunities"] = ConsolidatedOpportunities.split(',');
        jsonObject["OpportunityLoaded"] = OpportunityLoaded;
        return JSON.stringify(jsonObject);
    }

// DecodeReturnString(data) // returns parsed JSON string or undefined on error
    function DecodeReturnString(data)
    { 
        try
        { 
            return JSON.parse($("<div />").html(data).text());
        }
        catch (error)
        { 
            console.log(error.name);
            console.log(error.message);
            console.log(data);
        }
    }

// getUserContext() // returns void
    function getUserContext() {
        debugger;

    this.PreRate = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        }

// function PostRate(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostRate = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
       let tpb = $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').first();
      
      
      if ($(tpb).prop('checked') === false)  {
            $(tpb).checked = true;
            $(tpb).click();
            $(tpb).val('True');
        }
    }

    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        vm = this.vm;
        appendCSS();
        getUserContext();

        if (location === '/shipping') {
            //consigneeStateIsRequired = vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired;


            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                $terms = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms"]')
                $termsOfSale = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].TermsOfSale"]');

                var $consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]')
                consigneeState = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');
                consigneeCountry = $consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="Country"]');
                miscReference8 = $('[property="MiscReference8"] input');
                returnLabel = $('label:contains("Return Label")');
                returnOption = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]');

                var loaded = $terms.length && $termsOfSale.length && consigneeState.length &&
                consigneeCountry.length && miscReference8.length && returnLabel.length && returnOption.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    documentReady();
                }
            }, 50);
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        returnNameAddressCaption(false);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = theUsersName;
        if (consigneeStateIsRequired != undefined) {
            this.vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = consigneeStateIsRequired;
        }
    }

// documentReady() // returns void
    function documentReady() {
        $terms.add($termsOfSale).find("option:gt(0)").each(function (x, y) {
            if (y.value === 'string:CONSIGNEE') {
                y.label = 'Receiver';
            } else if (y.value == 'string:SHIPPER' || y.value === 'string:DDP') {
                y.label = 'UPS Account';
            } else {
                $(this).remove();
            }
        });

        consigneeCountry.change(function(e){
            setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement();
        });

        returnLabel.click(function(e) {
            var returnDelivery = vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery;
            var isReturn = returnDelivery == undefined || returnDelivery == true;
            returnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
        })

        returnOption.change(function(e) {
            returnNameAddressCaption(this.checked);
        })

        miscReference8.change(function(e) {
            var ref8 = $(this).val();
            if (/\d+/i.test(ref8)) {
                if (!/\d+kgs/i.test(ref8)) {
                    var match = ref8.match(/^[\d.]+/);
                    $(this).val(match[0] + "kgs").change()
                }
            }
        })

    }

// ajaxGet(url) // returns the AJAX response result
function ajaxGet(url) {
    var result;
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: url,
        async: false,
        success: function(response) {
            result = response;
        }
    });
    return result;
}

// getUserName() // returns the extracted user email string
     function getUserName() {
        var helloUser = $('a[title="Manage"]:contains("Hello")').text();
        return helloUser.match(/[a-zA-Z]+[a-zA-Z0-9._]+@[a-zA-Z]+\.[a-zA-Z.]{2,5}/i)[0];
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         vm = this.vm;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User", shipmentRequest);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User", shipmentRequest);
    };

// GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) // returns string
this.GetCustom = function(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        }
        if (customDataType === "To") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        }

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;

    };

// function UserMethod(logoNumber) // returns void
    function UserMethod(logoNumber) {

		if (logoNumber == 4) {

			var orderNumber = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').val();

			if (orderNumber === undefined || orderNumber === null || orderNumber === "") {

				client.alert.Danger("Missing or invalid Order Number, no update made.  Please enter a valid order number and try again.");
			}
			else {
			
				var usermethodParams = { "action": 4, "orderNumber": orderNumber, "percentageComplete":"0", "trailerNumber":"", "shipper":""};
				var results;
				var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
				var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
					if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
						client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
					} else {
						results = response["Data"];
					}
				});
				
				
				/*$.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
                    async: false,
                    cache: false,
                    dataType: "json",
                    data: { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) },
                    success: function(response) {
                        results = response["Data"];
                        ;
                    },
                    error: function (error) {
                        alert("Finalize Shipment has failed, no update made to the system.  Contact Support.");
                    }
                });*/
			}
		}
		else {

			$("#fileLoader").click();

			var encodedBase64Logo;

			var filesSelected = document.getElementById("fileLoader").files;

			if (filesSelected.length > 0) {
				var fileToLoad = filesSelected[0];

				var fileReader = new FileReader();

				fileReader.readAsDataURL(fileToLoad);

				fileReader.onload = function (event) {
					var encodedBase64Logo = logoNumber + event.target.result;

					SoxOnWcfDblHop.userMethod(encodedBase64Logo,
						function (result) {
							// Do something with the data

							DisplayLogoSaveMessage(result);

						},
						function (e) {
							// Do something with the error

							alert(e.message);
						});
				};
			}
		}
	}

// this.PageInitialize(viewModel) // returns undefined
    this.PageInitialize = function(viewModel) {
        vm = viewModel;
        //console.log(client.userContext);
        var searchCriteria = {WhereClauses:[{ FieldName:"Name", FieldValue:"Company Address Book", Operator:0 }]};
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
        //var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, SearchCriteria: searchCriteria };
        
		//debugger;
		
        $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
        {
            //console.log('response from inside method: ', response);

            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
            {
                var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
    
                data = { UserContext: client.userContext, AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
                //console.log(data);
                
                $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
                {
                    //console.log(response);
                    if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
                    {
                        tpbAddressBookEntries = response.AddressBookEntries;
                        vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes = tpbAddressBookEntries;
                    }                    
                    //debugger;
                }));
            }
        }));

    };

            {
                var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
    
                data = { UserContext: client.userContext, AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
                //console.log(data);
                
                $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
                {
                    //console.log(response);
                    if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
                    {
                        tpbAddressBookEntries = response.AddressBookEntries;
                        vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes = tpbAddressBookEntries;
                    }                    
                    debugger;
                }));
            }
        }));

    };

// function PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
        
        if (this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== undefined){
                 this.GetWeight(); 
        }
        
        //alert(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Amount);
        userParams.cbrWeight = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Amount;

        
        loadValue = loadValue.trim();
        var validate = validateOrderValue(loadValue);
        if (validate === "EMPTY") {
            alert("LOAD VALUE REQUIRED PLEASE");
        }
        userParams.orderType = validate;   
        console.log(userParams);
       
    };

// function GetWeight() // returns void
this.GetWeight = function () {
        if (this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== null) {
           
            var url = "https://localhost:5001/api/Scale/Read";
            var data ={
                "PortType": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                "Port": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.Port,
                "UsbVid": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                "UsbPid": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                "RequestCommand": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                "StopBits": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                "Parity": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                "RequestTimeout": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                "HostAddress": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.HostAddress,
                "RegexPattern": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                "DeviceParser": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                "DeviceName": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                "Handshake": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Handshake
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            //debugger;
            console.log(data);
            console.log(ret);
            
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                
                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": "LB"
                };
               
                if (ret.HasDimensions) {
                    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].Dimensions = {
                        "Length": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[0],
                        "Width": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[1],
                        "Height": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[2],
                        //"Units": ret.DimensionUnit.toUpperCase() === "IN" ? 0 : 1
                        "Units": "In"
                    };
                }
            }
        }
    };

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        if (sbrMessage(shipmentRequest)) {
            alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
        }
    };

// Source: Worldwide Cargo Services Inc (WORLDWIDECSI)_API TEST_1781.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        if (location === '/shipping')
            this.Shipping();
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.profile.Services.sort(byService);

        $(client.shipping.buildShipmentModal).on('shown.bs.modal', function () {
            client.shipping.buildTotalPackagesFocus();
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[name="postalCode"]', 'keydown', this.vm, postalCodeLookUp)

        function byService(a, b) {
            var sortingArr = [
                "UPS Next Day Air EAM (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Next Day Air (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Next Day Air Saver (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Second Day Air AM (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Second Day Air (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Three-Day Select (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Ground (UPS Adapter)"
            ]
            return sortingArr.indexOf(a.Name) - sortingArr.indexOf(b.Name);
        }

        function postalCodeLookUp(e) {
            var nameAddress = $(this).parents('name-address');
            e.data.addressName = nameAddress.attr('address-property-name');
            if (e.data.addressName == "Consignee" || e.data.addressName == "ReturnAddress") {
                var keyEvent = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keyEvent == 13 || keyEvent == 9) {
                    var city = nameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                    var stateProvince = nameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');
                    var postalCode = $(this).val();
                    if ((city.val() == '' || stateProvince.val() == '') && postalCode != '') {
                        $(client.shipping.cbrPostalCodeLookup).click();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

// BuildShipment(ret) // returns void
    this.BuildShipment = function (ret) {
        client.shipping.buildShipmentModalHide();

        var weightPerPackage;
        var multiPackage = this.currentShipment.Packages.length > 1;

        if (ret.TotalWeight !== undefined && ret.TotalWeight !== 0 && ret.TotalWeight !== "")
            weightPerPackage = (ret.TotalWeight / ret.TotalPackages).toFixed(3);

        for (var i = 0; i < ret.TotalPackages; i++) {
            this.packageIndex = this.currentShipment.Packages.length - 1;
            if (i > 0 || multiPackage) {
                this.addPackage();
                multiPackage = true;
            }

            if (weightPerPackage !== undefined)
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Amount = weightPerPackage;
            if (ret.WeightUnit !== undefined)
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Units = ret.WeightUnit;
            else
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Units = this.translations.WeightUnit;
        }
        this.totalPackages = this.currentShipment.Packages.length;

        ret.TotalWeight = '';
        ret.TotalPackages = '';
    }

// PostalCodeLookup(addressName) // returns void
    this.PostalCodeLookup = function (addressName) {
debugger;
        var userContext = this.getUserContext(this);
        var postalCode = $('[address-property-name="' + addressName + '"] [name="postalCode"]').val();
        var content = { AddressName: addressName, PostalCode: postalCode };
        var payload = { Action: 'CSZ', Content: JSON.stringify(content) };
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(payload), UserContext: userContext };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.ErrorCode > 0) {
            client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', response.ErrorMessage)
        } else {
            var responseData = JSON.parse(client.htmlText(response.Data));        
            if (responseData == null) {
                client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', 'Invalid or Not US Postal Code');
            } else {
                if (responseData.length > 1) {
                    this.addressResults = responseData;
                    client.shipping.validateAddressModalShow();
                } else {
                    this.currentShipment.updateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, responseData[0].City, responseData[0].StateProvince)
                }
            }
        }
    }

// UpdateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, city, stateProvince) // returns void
    this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ = function (addressName, city, stateProvince) {
        var nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'ReturnAddress') {
            if (this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress == undefined)
                this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {};
            nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress;
        }
        nameAddress.City = city;
        nameAddress.StateProvince = stateProvince;
    }

// SelectAddress(address) // returns void
    this.SelectAddress = function (address) {
        client.shipping.validateAddressModalHide();
        this.updateNameAddressCSZ(address.AddressName, address.City, address.StateProvince);
    }

// CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns void
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {            
            event.preventDefault();
debugger;
            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');
            var createShipmentInput = '#buildShipmentModalBody input';

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // allow shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }

        function isInputsEmpty($inputs) {
            var inputsIsEmpty = false;
            $inputs.each(function () {
                if (this.type == 'text') {
                    if (this.value.trim() == "") {
                        this.focus();
                        inputsIsEmpty = true;
                        return false;
                    };
                };
            });
            return inputsIsEmpty;
        }
    }

// GetUserContext(vm) // returns userContext or UserInformation
    this.GetUserContext = function (vm) {
        if (vm.userContext) return vm.userContext;
        if (vm.UserInformation) return vm.UserInformation;
    }

// ThinClientAPIRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns jqXHR response from $.post
    this.ThinClientAPIRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = client.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = client.getAuthorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken })
    }
